# <a name="quality-of-experience-review-guide"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-103">体验质量检查指南</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-103">Quality of Experience Review Guide</span></span> 

<!-- Note that this link to the Word doc is intentionally NOT the aka.ms/qerquide link -->
<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-104">本指南介绍 Microsoft 团队和 Skype for business Online 的 "驱动器价值" 阶段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-104">This guide is about the Drive Value phase for Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business Online.</span></span> 

## <a name="introduction"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-105">简介</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-105">Introduction</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-106">为了对改善用户体验的最大影响，组织需要 operationalize 下图中所示的关键区域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-106">To have the greatest impact on improving the user experience, organizations need to operationalize the key areas that are shown in the following figure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-107">其他方面包括确定操作任务、确定质量标准的目标、ascertaining 用于衡量组织成功的衡量标准，以及根据需要缩小调查的范围。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-107">Additional areas include identifying operational tasks, establishing targets for quality metrics, ascertaining the metrics to use to gauge organizational success, and narrowing areas of investigation as needed.</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-108">![用户体验质量的关键领域](media/qerguide-image-keyareas.png "用户体验质量的关键领域包括音频、可靠性、用户调查、设备和客户端。")</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-108">![Key areas for the quality of user experience](media/qerguide-image-keyareas.png "Key areas for the quality of user experience include audio, reliability, user surveys, devices, and clients.")</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-109">_图 1-本指南中涵盖的关键操作区域_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-109">_Figure 1 - Key operational areas covered throughout this guide_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-110">通过不断评估和修正本指南中所述的区域，你可以降低对用户体验质量产生负面影响的可能性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-110">By continually assessing and remediating the areas described in this guide, you can reduce their potential to negatively affect the quality of your users' experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-111">在部署中遇到的大多数用户体验问题可以分为以下类别：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-111">Most user-experience problems encountered in a deployment can be grouped into the following categories:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-112">防火墙或代理配置不完整</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-112">Incomplete firewall or proxy configuration</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-113">Wi-Fi 覆盖范围较小</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-113">Poor Wi-Fi coverage</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-114">带宽不足</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-114">Insufficient bandwidth</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-115">VPN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-115">VPN</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-116">不一致或过时的客户端版本和驱动程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-116">Inconsistent or outdated client versions and drivers</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-117">未优化或内置音频设备</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-117">Unoptimized or built-in audio devices</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-118">子网或网络设备存在问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-118">Problematic subnets or network devices</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-119">通过在部署团队或 Skype for business Online 之前制定正确的规划和设计，你可以减少保持高质量体验所需的工作量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-119">Through proper planning and design before deploying Teams or Skype for Business Online, you can reduce the amount of effort that will be required to maintain high-quality experiences.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-120">本指南重点介绍使用 "呼叫质量" 仪表板（CQD）作为主要工具来报告和调查每个区域，并对音频进行特殊强调以最大程度地提高采纳和影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-120">This guide focuses on using the Call Quality Dashboard (CQD) Online as the primary tool to report and investigate each area, with a special emphasis on audio to maximize adoption and impact.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-121">对网络进行的改进音频体验的任何改进也将直接转换为视频和桌面共享中的改进。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-121">Any improvements made to the network to improve the audio experience will also directly translate to improvements in video and desktop sharing.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-122">为加速评估，提供了[两个特选 CQD 模板](https://aka.ms/qertemplates)：一个用于管理所有网络，另一个仅针对托管（内部）网络进行筛选。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-122">To accelerate your assessment, [two curated CQD templates](https://aka.ms/qertemplates) are provided: one is for managing all networks and the other is filtered for managed (internal) networks only.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-123">虽然 "所有网络" 模板报表配置为显示建筑物和网络信息，但在您处理收集和上载建筑物信息时仍可使用这些报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-123">Although the All Networks template reports are configured to display building and network information, they can still be used while you work toward collecting and uploading building information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-124">将生成信息上载到 CQD 使服务可以通过添加自定义建筑物、网络和位置信息来增强报告，同时区分外部子网的内部子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-124">Uploading building information into CQD enables the service to enhance reporting by adding custom building, network, and location information while differentiating internal from external subnets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-125">有关详细信息，请参阅本指南后面的[构建地图](#building-mapping)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-125">For more information, see [Building mapping](#building-mapping) later in this guide.</span></span>

### <a name="intended-audience"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-126">目标受众</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-126">Intended audience</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-127">本指南旨在供合作伙伴和客户利益干系人使用，其角色包括协作领导/架构师、顾问、变更管理/采纳专家、支持/技术支持人员、网络主管、桌面组长和 IT 管理员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-127">This guide is intended to be used by partner and customer stakeholders with roles such as Collaboration Lead/Architect, Consultant, Change Management/Adoption Specialist, Support/Help Desk Lead, Network Lead, Desktop Lead, and IT Admin.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-128">本指南还旨在供指定的质量专家使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-128">This guide is also intended to be used by the designated quality champion(s).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-129">有关详细信息，请参阅[质量拥护者角色](4-envision-plan-my-service-management.md#the-quality-champion-role)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-129">For more information, see [the Quality Champion role](4-envision-plan-my-service-management.md#the-quality-champion-role).</span></span>

## <a name="assign-roles-for-accessing-cqd"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-130">为访问 CQD 分配角色</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-130">Assign roles for accessing CQD</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-131">使用本指南之前，请确保你已分配正确的租户[角色](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/admin/add-users/about-admin-roles)，以便你可以访问 CQD。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-131">Before using this guide, make sure you have the proper tenant [roles](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/admin/add-users/about-admin-roles) assigned so that you can access CQD.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-132">下表显示了每个角色在 CQD 中可以执行的操作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-132">This table shows you what each role can do in CQD:</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-178">如果您没有看到 EUII （最终用户的可识别信息），并且您拥有允许查看此信息的角色之一，请记住 CQD 仅保留30天的 EUII。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-178">If you're not seeing EUII (end-user identifiable information) and you have one of the roles that's permitted to see this information, keep in mind that CQD only keeps EUII for 30 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-179">将删除30天之前的任何内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-179">Anything older than 30 days is deleted.</span></span>

## <a name="what-is-quality"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-180">什么是质量？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-180">What is quality?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-181">在团队和 Skype for business 中讨论质量时，定义术语以实现共同的理解非常重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-181">When discussing quality in Teams and Skype for Business, it's important to define the term to achieve a common understanding.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-182">在此处定义的质量是服务指标和用户体验的组合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-182">Quality, as defined here, is a combination of service metrics and user experience.</span></span>

<!-- Note: need to update graphic-->
<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-183">![服务指标和用户体验的插图](media/qerguide-image-whatisquality.png "服务指标由较差的流比率、可靠性、终结点/设备和客户端版本组成。用户体验由用户对服务质量的理解构成。")</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-183">![Illustration of service metrics and the user experience](media/qerguide-image-whatisquality.png "Service metrics are made up of poor stream ratio, reliability, endpoints/devices, and client versions. The user experience is made up of the user's perception of the quality of the service.")</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-184">_图 2-什么是质量？_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-184">_Figure 2 - What is quality?_</span></span>

### <a name="service-metrics"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-185">服务指标</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-185">Service metrics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-186">服务指标由基于客户端的特定指标组成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-186">Service metrics consist of specific client-based metrics.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-187">在每次通话期间，客户将收集有关呼叫的遥测信息，并在每次调用结束时提交报告，以后可通过 CQD 或[调用分析](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309)进行访问。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-187">During each call, the client collects telemetry information about the call and submits a report at the end of each call that can be later accessed through CQD or [Call Analytics](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-188">这些指标包括：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-188">These metrics include:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-189">较差的流速率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-189">Poor Stream Rate</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-190">设置失败率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-190">Setup Failure Rate</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-191">丢单故障率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-191">Drop Failure Rate</span></span>


#### <a name="poor-stream-rate"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-192">较差的流速率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-192">Poor Stream Rate</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-193">较差的流速率（PSR.EXE）表示组织的质量较差的流的总体百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-193">The poor stream rate (PSR) represents the organization's overall percentage of streams that have poor quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-194">此指标旨在突出显示你的组织集中关注的区域，以达到降低此值和改善用户体验的最大影响，这是在查看 PSR.EXE 时[托管网络](#managed-vs-unmanaged-networks)的主要焦点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-194">This metric is meant to highlight areas where your organization can concentrate effort to have the strongest impact toward reducing this value and improving the user experience, which is why [managed networks](#managed-vs-unmanaged-networks) are the primary focus when looking at PSR.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-195">外部用户也很重要，但调查在组织的基础上有所不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-195">External users are important too, but investigation differs on an organizational basis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-196">考虑为外部用户提供最佳做法，并独立于整个组织调查外部呼叫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-196">Consider providing best practices for external users, and investigate external calls independently from the overall organization.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-197">CQD 中的实际度量值因工作负荷而异，但为了使质量体验进行评审，我们主要关注_音频的差百分比_度量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-197">The actual measurement in CQD varies by workload, but for the purposes of the Quality Experience Review we focus primarily on the _Audio Poor Percentage_ measurement.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-198">PSR.EXE 是由下表中所述的五个网络度量值组成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-198">PSR is made up of the five network metric averages described in the following table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-199">对于要归类为较差的流，只有一个指标需要超过所定义的阈值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-199">For a stream to be classified as poor, only one metric needs to exceed the defined threshold.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-200">有关流分类过程的详细信息，请参阅[本文](stream-classification-in-call-quality-dashboard.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-200">For more information about the stream classification process, see [this article](stream-classification-in-call-quality-dashboard.md).</span></span>

> [!Note]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-201">CQD 提供 "不太好的原因 ..."测量，以便更好地了解导致流归为差的条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-201">CQD provides the "Poor Due To…" measurements to better understand what condition caused the stream to be classified as poor.</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-202">_表 1-音频质量不佳的指标_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-202">_Table 1 - Audio poor quality metrics_</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-203">平均指标</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-203">Metric average</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-204">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-204">Description</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-205">用户体验</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-205">User experience</span></span> |
|-------------|-----------------|-----------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-206">抖动\>30 毫秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-206">Jitter \>30 ms</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-207">这是连续数据包之间的延迟的平均变化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-207">This is the average change in delay between successive packets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-208">团队和 Skype for business 可以通过缓冲来适应某些级别的抖动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-208">Teams and Skype for Business can adapt to some levels of jitter through buffering.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-209">仅当抖动超过的是参与者注意到抖动效果的缓冲时才会如此。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-209">It's only when the jitter exceeds the buffering that a participant notices the effects of jitter.</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-210">以不同的速度收到的数据包将使扬声器的语音与声音机器人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-210">The packets arriving at different speeds cause a speaker's voice to sound robotic.</span></span>   |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-211">数据包丢失率\>10% 或0。1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-211">Packet loss rate \>10% or 0.1</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-212">这通常定义为丢失的数据包的百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-212">This is often defined as a percentage of packets that are lost.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-213">数据包丢失直接影响音频质量-从少量的单个丢失的数据包，几乎不影响对导致音频完全减少的后端到后突发损失的影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-213">Packet loss directly affects audio quality—from small, individual lost packets that have almost no impact to back-to-back burst losses that cause audio to cut out completely.</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-214">数据包被丢弃且未到达其预期目标会导致媒体出现间隙，导致丢失音节和单词，并且视频和共享断断续续。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-214">The packets being dropped and not arriving at their intended destination cause gaps in the media, resulting in missed syllables and words, and choppy video and sharing.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-215">往返时间\>500 ms</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-215">Round-trip time \>500 ms</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-216">这是将 IP 数据包从点 A 转到点 B 并返回到点 A 所需的时间。此网络传播延迟与两个点之间的物理距离和光之间的距离密切相关，并且包括网络路径中的各种设备所占用的额外开销。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-216">This is the time it takes to get an IP packet from point A to point B and back to point A. This network propagation delay is tied to the physical distance between the two points and the speed of light, and includes additional overhead taken by the various devices in the network path.</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-217">数据包到达目的地的时间太长，导致 walkie talkie 效果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-217">The packets taking too long to arrive at their destination cause a walkie-talkie effect.</span></span>   |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-218">NMOS 下降平均\>1。0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-218">NMOS degradation average \>1.0</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-219">流的平均[网络平均观点（NMOS）](https://docs.microsoft.com/previous-versions/office/communications-server/bb894481(v=office.12)#network-mos)性能下降。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-219">Average [Network Mean Opinion Score (NMOS)](https://docs.microsoft.com/previous-versions/office/communications-server/bb894481(v=office.12)#network-mos) degradation for the stream.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-220">表示网络损失和抖动对导致 NMOS 通过多个点丢弃的已接收音频的质量有多大的影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-220">Represents how much the network loss and jitter has affected the quality of received audio that caused the NMOS to drop by more than one point.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-221">这是抖动、数据包丢失和较低级别的组合——延长往返时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-221">This is a combination of jitter, packet loss, and—to a lesser degree—increased round-trip time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-222">用户可能遇到这些症状的组合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-222">The user might be experiencing a combination of these symptoms.</span></span>   |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-223">隐藏样本\>7% 或0.07 的平均比率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-223">Average ratio of concealed samples \>7% or 0.07</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-224">带有隐藏样本（由数据包丢失修复生成）到音频帧总数的音频帧数的平均比率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-224">Average ratio of the number of audio frames with concealed samples generated by packet loss healing to the total number of audio frames.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-225">隐藏的音频示例是一种技术，用于平滑通常由丢弃网络数据包导致的突然过渡。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-225">A concealed audio sample is a technique used to smooth out the abrupt transition that would usually be caused by dropped network packets.</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-226">高值表示应用了严重级别的损失 concealment，并导致音频失真。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-226">High values indicate that significant levels of loss concealment were applied and resulted in distorted or lost audio.</span></span>     |

#### <a name="setup-failure-rate"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-227">设置失败率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-227">Setup Failure Rate</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-228">设置失败率（在 CQD 中称为 "_总呼叫设置失败百分比_测量"）表示在呼叫开始时终结点之间无法建立媒体路径的流的数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-228">The setup failure rate, otherwise known as the _Total Call Setup Failure Percentage_ measurement in CQD, is the number of streams where the media path couldn't be established between the endpoints at the start of the call.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-229">这表示无法建立的任何媒体流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-229">This represents any media stream that couldn't be established.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-230">根据此处测量的用户体验影响的严重程度，目标是将此值尽可能缩小到零。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-230">Given the severity of the impact on the user experience measured here, the goal is to reduce this value to as close to zero as possible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-231">在具有不完整的防火墙规则的新部署中，此指标的高值在防火墙规则上比成熟部署更常见，但仍需要定期观看非常重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-231">A high value for this metric is more common in new deployments with incomplete firewall rules than a mature deployment, but it's still important to watch on a regular basis.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-232">此指标的计算方法是使用已提交成功呼叫详细记录（CDR）的流总数设置的失败流总数：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-232">This metric is calculated by taking the total number of streams that failed to set up divided by the total number of streams that submitted a successful call detail record (CDR):</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-233">**设置失败率**= 总通话设置失败流计数/总 CDR 可用流计数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-233">**Setup Failure Rate** = Total Call Setup Failed Stream Count / Total CDR Available Stream Count</span></span>

#### <a name="drop-failure-rate"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-234">丢单故障率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-234">Drop Failure Rate</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-235">在 CQD 中，"丢弃故障率" （也称为 "_总通话中断失败百分比_度量值"）是已成功建立媒体路径但未正常终止的流的百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-235">The drop failure rate, otherwise known as the _Total Call Dropped Failure Percentage_ measurement in CQD, is the percentage of successfully established streams where the media path didn't terminate normally.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-236">这表示意外终止的任何媒体流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-236">This represents any media stream that terminated unexpectedly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-237">尽管这种影响不会像设置失败的流那样严重，但会对用户体验产生负面影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-237">Although the impact of this isn't as severe as a stream that failed to set up, it will negatively affect the user experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-238">突然和频繁的媒体丢弃不仅会对用户体验产生严重影响，还会导致用户需要重新连接，从而导致生产力损失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-238">Sudden and frequent media drops not only can have a severe impact on the user experience, they result in the need for users to reconnect, resulting in a loss in productivity.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-239">通过将丢弃流的总数除以已成功设置的流的总数来计算指标：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-239">The metric is calculated by taking the total number of dropped streams divided by the total count of streams that set up successfully:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-240">**丢单失败率**= 总通话中断流计数/总通话设置成功流计数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-240">**Drop Failure Rate** = Total Call Dropped Stream Count / Total Call Setup Succeeded Stream Count</span></span>

### <a name="define-your-target-metrics"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-241">定义目标指标</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-241">Define your target metrics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-242">本部分将讨论一些核心服务指标，这些指标用于评估服务体验运行状况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-242">This section discusses some of the core service metrics that we use to assess how services experience health.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-243">通过不断评估和推动将这些指标保留在其定义的目标之下，你将帮助确保你的用户体验一致、可靠的通话质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-243">By continually assessing and driving efforts to keep these metrics below their defined targets, you'll help ensure that your users experience consistent, reliable call quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-244">为此，我们提供了以下目标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-244">To get you started, the following targets are provided.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-245">_表 2-核心目标运行状况评估指标_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-245">_Table 2 - Core target health assessment metrics_</span></span>

</table>


<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-299">讨论和定义组织的目标以满足您的业务目标非常重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-299">It's important to discuss and define your organization's targets to meet your business objectives.</span></span>

### <a name="user-experience"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-300">用户体验</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-300">User experience</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-301">分析用户体验比科学更是更多的艺术，因为此处收集的指标并不总是意味着网络或服务存在问题，而是指示用户感觉问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-301">Analyzing the user experience is more art than science, because the metrics gathered here don't always mean that there's a problem with the network or service but rather, they simply indicate that the user perceives a problem.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-302">Microsoft 提供了一种内置的调查机制（称为 "我的呼叫费率" （RMC））来帮助评估整体用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-302">Microsoft offers a built-in survey mechanism—known as Rate My Call (RMC)—to help gauge overall user experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-303">RMC 将帮助你从用户的视角回答以下问题：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-303">RMC will help you answer the following questions from your users' perspective:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-304">我知道如何使用该解决方案？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-304">Do I know how to use the solution?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-305">该解决方案是否易于使用和直观，并且它是否支持我的日常通讯需求？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-305">Is the solution easy to use and intuitive, and does it support my day-to-day communication needs?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-306">该解决方案是否可帮助我完成作业？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-306">Does the solution help me get my job done?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-307">对解决方案的总体理解有哪些？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-307">What's my overall perception of the solution?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-308">是否可以在任何时间点使用该解决方案，无论我在哪里？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-308">Can I use the solution at any point in time, regardless of where I am?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-309">是否可以设置和维护呼叫？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-309">Can I set up and maintain a call?</span></span>

#### <a name="rate-my-call"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-310">评价我的呼叫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-310">Rate My Call</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-311">费率我的通话费率（RMC）内置于团队和 Skype for business 中，并自动配置为在每10次通话中一次或10% 的参与者显示给参与者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-311">Rate My Call (RMC) is built into Teams and Skype for Business and is automatically configured to be displayed to the participant after one in every 10 calls, or 10 percent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-312">此简短调查要求用户对呼叫进行评级，并提供有关通话质量可能较差的小环境。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-312">This brief survey asks the user to rate the call and provide a little context for why the call quality might have been poor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-313">一个或两个等级被视为差，3到4是好的，5为极佳。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-313">A one or two rating is considered poor, three to four is good, and five is excellent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-314">尽管它有些滞后指示器，但这是发现服务指标可能遗漏的问题的有用指标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-314">Although it's somewhat of a lagging indicator, this is a useful metric for uncovering issues that service metrics can miss.</span></span>

> [!Note]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-315">在用户通过提供较好的反馈 RMC 调查来响应调查时，回复通常会返回 overwhelmingly 负数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-315">Until users are educated to respond to RMC surveys by giving good feedback in addition to bad, responses typically come back as overwhelmingly negative.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-316">当通话质量较差时，大多数用户仅响应。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-316">Most users only respond when call quality is poor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-317">因此，即使服务指标良好，你的 RMC 报表也可能会倾斜到差的一边。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-317">Because of this, your RMC reports might be skewed to the poor side even while service metrics are good.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-318">你可以使用 CQD 来报告 RMC 用户答复，并且示例报表包含在 CQD 模板中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-318">You can use CQD to report on RMC user responses, and sample reports are included in the CQD template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-319">但是，本指南中不详细介绍它们。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-319">However, they aren't discussed in detail in this guide.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-320">有关 Skype for Business Online RMC 和指导用户提供有用的 RMC 响应的详细信息，请参阅[此博客文章](https://blogs.technet.microsoft.com/jenstr/2015/05/05/rate-my-call-in-skype-for-business-2015/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-320">For more information about RMC in Skype for Business Online and guidance for educating users to give useful RMC responses, see [this blog post](https://blogs.technet.microsoft.com/jenstr/2015/05/05/rate-my-call-in-skype-for-business-2015/).</span></span>

#### <a name="client-and-device-readiness"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-321">客户端和设备准备情况</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-321">Client and device readiness</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-322">你需要一个可靠的客户端和设备策略，以帮助确保你的用户具有一致且积极的用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-322">You need a solid client and device strategy to help ensure that your users have a consistent and positive user experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-323">一些关键原则推动了每个准备策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-323">A few key principles drive each readiness strategy.</span></span>

##### <a name="client-readiness"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-324">客户端就绪</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-324">Client readiness</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-325">强大的客户端准备策略可确保用户运行最新版本的客户端，同时享受最佳体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-325">A strong client readiness strategy ensures that your users are running the most recent version of the client while enjoying the best experience possible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-326">Microsoft 定期修补 Skype for Business 客户端;确保你的环境中的最新状态是你的整体成功的关键。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-326">Microsoft routinely patches the Skype for Business client; ensuring that you keep it up to date in your environment is vital to your overall success.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-327">记住修补网络、视频、USB 和音频驱动程序也很重要，因为它们经常被忽视，并且可能会影响用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-327">It's also important to remember to patch network, video, USB, and audio drivers, because they're often overlooked and can affect the user's experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-328">考虑将网络、Wlan、视频、USB 和音频驱动程序添加到你的当前修补程序管理过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-328">Consider adding network, Wi-Fi, video, USB, and audio drivers to your current patch management process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-329">我们建议你不要让你的客户端版本低于6个月。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-329">We recommend that you not let your client versions fall behind by more than six months.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-330">如果您使用的是 Office 即点即用，则该服务已随时保持最新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-330">If you're using Office Click-to-Run, you're already being kept up to date by the service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-331">如本指南后面所述，使用随附的[客户端版本](#client-versions)来帮助您完成此过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-331">Use the included [client versions](#client-versions), as described later in this guide, to assist you with this process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-332">您还可以利用 "我的通话" 示例报告来进一步增强您的客户准备策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-332">You can also leverage the Rate My Call sample reports to further enhance your client readiness strategy.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-333">当前，团队客户通过 Azure 内容交付网络自动分发和更新，并将由服务保持最新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-333">Currently, Teams clients are distributed and updated automatically through the Azure Content Delivery Network and will be kept up to date by the service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-334">因此，客户准备和调查活动不适用于团队。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-334">Due to this, client readiness and investigative activities aren't applicable to Teams.</span></span>


##### <a name="device-readiness"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-335">设备准备就绪</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-335">Device readiness</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-336">任何一个策略都不会影响用户体验，而不仅仅是设备准备策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-336">No one single strategy can affect the user experience more than your device readiness strategy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-337">大多数组织都很乐意从用户那里删除不必要的设备（例如桌面电话或其他专用音频设备），这通常是切换到团队或 Skype for business 的核心业务理由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-337">Most organizations are happy to remove unnecessary devices (for example, desk phones or other dedicated audio devices) from users, and this is often a core business justification for switching to Teams or Skype for Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-338">但是，这些相同的组织有时也可以提供替代设备，即使这些设备成本较低。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-338">However, those same organizations sometimes hesitate to provide replacement devices, even if those devices are less expensive.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-339">虽然配备内置麦克风和扬声器的新式笔记本电脑和电脑没有针对企业级语音语音（VoIP）进行优化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-339">Modern-day laptops and PCs, though equipped with built-in microphone and speaker, aren't optimized for business-class voice over IP (VoIP).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-340">这通常会为所有参与者带来不好的体验，尤其是当扬声器处于噪音环境中时。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-340">This often creates a poor experience for all participants, especially if the speaker is in a noisy environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-341">Microsoft 的设备认证计划可确保当用户通过使用针对团队或 Skype for business 认证的任何设备参与电话呼叫时，它将产生一个与非认证设备更出色的体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-341">Microsoft's device certification program ensures that when a user participates in a phone call by using any device certified for Teams or Skype for Business, it produces an experience that's superior to a non-certified device.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-342">我们始终建议团队和 Skype for business 用户在通过桌面客户端参与语音呼叫时使用已认证的耳机或扬声器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-342">We always recommend that Teams and Skype for Business users use a certified headset or speaker when participating in a voice call through the desktop client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-343">有关 Microsoft 认证的设备的详细信息，请查看有关[认证计划](/SkypeForBusiness/certification/overview)和查看[合作伙伴解决方案目录](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs)的这些文章。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-343">For more information about Microsoft certified devices, review these articles about the [certification program](/SkypeForBusiness/certification/overview) and view the [partner solutions catalog](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-344">使用本指南后面所述的 "[设备" 报告](#devices)，获取有关管理设备的帮助。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-344">Use the [Devices report](#devices), described later in this guide, for assistance with managing your devices.</span></span>


### <a name="categories-of-quality"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-345">质量类别</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-345">Categories of quality</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-346">Operationalizing 高质量和可靠部署的成功与否取决于你的构建运行严格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-346">The success of operationalizing a high-quality and reliable deployment depends on your building operational rigor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-347">尤其要特别注意下图中所示的三个类别;以下是本指南的重点：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-347">Specifically, pay special attention to the three categories illustrated in the following figure; these are the focus of this guide:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-348">**网络：** 音频质量重点针对不良流比率（PSR.EXE）指标、TCP 使用、有线和无线子网以及标识 HTTP 代理和 VPN 的使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-348">**Network:** Audio quality focused on the Poor Stream Ratio (PSR) metric, TCP usage, wired and wireless subnets, and identifying the use of HTTP proxies and VPN.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-349">**终结点：** 音频设备和客户端版本（仅 Skype for business）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-349">**Endpoints:** Audio devices and client versions (Skype for Business only).</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-350">**服务管理：** 此类别包含两个部分：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-350">**Service Management:** This category comprises two sections:</span></span>

    -   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-351">首先，Microsoft 有责任管理和维护团队和 Skype for business Online 服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-351">First is Microsoft's responsibility to manage and maintain the Teams and Skype for Business Online services.</span></span>

    -   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-352">第二是组织必须管理的任务以确保能够可靠地访问该服务，例如，在将基础结构添加到服务中时，更新构建信息和维护新 Office 365 IP 地址的防火墙。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-352">Second are tasks your organization must manage to ensure reliable access to the service, such as updating building information and maintaining firewalls for new Office 365 IP addresses as infrastructure is added to the service.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-353">![组织中质量类别的图形](media/qerguide-image-categories.png "组织中的质量类别：服务管理、终结点和网络。")</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-353">![Graph of the categories of quality in an organization](media/qerguide-image-categories.png "The categories of quality in an organization: service management, endpoints, and the network.")</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-354">_图 3-团队和 Skype for business Online 部署的关键类别_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-354">_Figure 3 - Critical categories for Teams and Skype for Business Online deployment_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-355">下图介绍了每个类别必须执行的任务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-355">The following graphic outlines the tasks you must execute for each category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-356">我们建议您至少每周运行一次这些任务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-356">We recommend that you run these tasks once a week, at a minimum.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-357">第一次执行这些任务比后续迭代需要更多的工作，因为其中许多类别都要求您验证部署配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-357">The first time you perform these tasks will take more effort than subsequent iterations, because many of these categories require that you validate your deployment configurations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-358">通过满足你定义的目标实现所需的状态后，执行这些任务将帮助你维护该状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-358">After you've achieved the state you want by meeting the targets you've defined, performing these tasks will help you maintain that state.</span></span>

<!--  This is a net new graphic, never was included in the online article. OOPS! -->
<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-359">![每个质量类别的每周任务列表](media/qerguide-image-tasks.png "每个质量类别的每周任务列表")</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-359">![List of weekly tasks per quality category](media/qerguide-image-tasks.png "List of weekly tasks per quality category")</span></span>

#### <a name="service-management-tasks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-360">服务管理任务</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-360">Service management tasks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-361">在 cloud-first world 中，你必须执行某些服务管理任务来保持高质量的用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-361">In a cloud-first world, you must perform certain service management tasks to maintain high-quality user experiences.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-362">这些任务范围包括：确保有足够的带宽来联系服务，但没有饱和 internet 链接，验证所有托管网络区域的服务质量（QoS）是否存在，并在防火墙上的[Office 365 IP 范围](https://aka.ms/o365ips)内保持最高。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-362">These tasks range from ensuring there is sufficient bandwidth to reach the service without saturating internet links, validating that quality of service (QoS) is in place on all managed network areas, and—lastly—staying on top of [Office 365 IP ranges on firewalls](https://aka.ms/o365ips).</span></span>

#### <a name="network-tasks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-363">网络任务</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-363">Network tasks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-364">网络任务有两种类别：可靠性和质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-364">There are two categories of network tasks: reliability and quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-365">可靠性侧重于衡量用户成功进行呼叫并保持连接的能力。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-365">Reliability focuses on measuring the user's ability to make calls successfully and stay connected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-366">质量重点介绍在呼叫期间和结束后，用户客户端发送给团队和 Skype for business Online 的聚合遥测。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-366">Quality focuses on the aggregated telemetry sent to Teams and Skype for Business Online by the user's client during the call and after it has ended.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-367">由于可靠性对用户体验有重大影响，因此在深入了解质量之前开始评估和调查这些指标非常重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-367">Given the critical impact that reliability has on the user experience, it's important to begin assessing and investigating those metrics before diving into quality.</span></span> 

#### <a name="endpoints-tasks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-368">终结点任务</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-368">Endpoints tasks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-369">此类别中的主要任务是验证哪些客户端版本在过去六个月内运行桌面版本的 Skype for Business，以确保用户获得对 Skype for business 桌面客户端的连续优化的好处。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-369">The main task in this category is validating which client versions are running Skype for Business on desktop builds from the last six months, to ensure users are getting the benefit of the continual optimizations made to the Skype for Business desktop client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-370">此外，这简化了整体客户端管理任务，并提供了一致的用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-370">Additionally, this simplifies overall client management tasks and provides a consistent user experience.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-371">另一个重要领域是监视哪些设备在你的部署中很流行，并推动使用已认证的设备来提供最佳用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-371">The other important area is monitoring which devices are prevalent in your deployment and driving the use of certified devices to provide the best user experience.</span></span>


> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-372">当前，团队客户通过 Azure 内容交付网络自动分发和更新，并将由服务保持最新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-372">Currently, Teams clients are distributed and updated automatically through the Azure Content Delivery Network and will be kept up to date by the service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-373">客户端准备情况和调查活动不适用于团队。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-373">Client readiness and investigative activities aren't applicable to Teams.</span></span>

## <a name="cqd-basics"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-374">CQD 基础知识</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-374">CQD basics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-375">本部分介绍使用 CQD 的基础知识。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-375">This section describes the fundamentals of working with CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-376">指南适用于以下主题：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-376">Guidance is given for the following topics:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-377">什么是 CQD？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-377">What is CQD?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-378">使用 CQD 的期望值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-378">Expectations using CQD</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-379">查找你的租户 ID</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-379">Finding your tenant ID</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-380">有关 Microsoft 团队和 Skype for Business 的报告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-380">Reporting on Microsoft Teams versus Skype for Business</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-381">第一和第二分类</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-381">First versus second classifications</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-382">维度、度量值和筛选器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-382">Dimensions, measures, and filters</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-383">流与通话</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-383">Streams versus calls</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-384">良好、差和未分类的通话</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-384">Good, poor, and unclassified calls</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-385">常见子网</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-385">Common subnets</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-386">有关更深入的培训和资源，请参阅[附录](#other-resources)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-386">For more in-depth training and resources, see the [Appendix](#other-resources).</span></span>

### <a name="what-is-cqd"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-387">什么是 CQD？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-387">What is CQD?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-388">使用呼叫质量仪表板（CQD）可深入了解使用团队和 Skype for business 服务进行的通话的质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-388">You use the Call Quality Dashboard (CQD) to gain insight into the quality of calls made by using Teams and Skype for Business services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-389">CQD 旨在帮助 Skype for business 和团队管理员和网络工程师优化网络，保持密切关注的质量、可靠性和用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-389">CQD is designed to help Skype for Business and Teams admins and network engineers optimize the network and keep a close eye on quality, reliability, and the user experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-390">CQD 查看整个组织的聚合遥测，其中整体模式可能会变得显而易见，使员工能够做出明智的评估和计划补救活动以最大限度地提高影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-390">CQD looks at aggregate telemetry for an entire organization where overall patterns can become apparent, allowing staff to make informed assessments and plan remediation activities to maximize impact.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-391">CQD 提供了有助于深入了解整体质量、可靠性和用户体验的指标的报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-391">CQD provides reports of metrics that provide insight into overall quality, reliability, and user experience.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-392">本指南将帮助您了解 CQD 的核心概念，以帮助最大程度地提高用户利用团队或 Skype for business 在线体验的影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-392">This guide will help in understanding the core concepts of CQD to help maximize the impact you can make in improving your users' experience with Teams or Skype for Business Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-393">在[附录](#other-resources)中可以找到其他 CQD 资源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-393">Additional CQD resources can be found in the [Appendix](#other-resources).</span></span>

### <a name="expectations-using-cqd"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-394">使用 CQD 的期望值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-394">Expectations using CQD</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-395">CQD 虽然对分析趋势和子网很有用，但并不总是为给定方案提供特定原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-395">CQD, although useful for analyzing trends and subnets, doesn't always provide a specific cause for a given scenario.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-396">在使用 CQD 时，了解这一点并设置正确的期望值非常重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-396">It's important to understand this and set the correct expectation when using CQD:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-397">CQD 不会为每个方案提供根本原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-397">CQD won't provide the root cause for every scenario.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-398">CQD 不能包含电话系统或音频会议流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-398">CQD won't contain Phone System or Audio Conferencing streams.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-399">CQD 将根据趋势分析要进一步调查的区域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-399">CQD will call out areas for further investigation based on trends.</span></span>

### <a name="report-editions"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-400">报表版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-400">Report editions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-401">CQD Online 中有两个报表版本： "摘要" 和 "详细信息"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-401">There are two report editions in CQD Online: Summary and Detailed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-402">使用位于屏幕顶部的栏中的下拉菜单打开报告版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-402">Use the drop-down menu located in the bar at the top of the screen to open a report edition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-403">所选报告版本的名称将显示在屏幕顶部。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-403">The name of the selected report edition is displayed at the top of the screen.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-404">摘要报表是静态报表，不能对其进行编辑、下载或导出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-404">Summary reports are static and can't be edited, downloaded, or exported.</span></span> 
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-405">详细报告可以完全自定义，并且可以下载到 CSV 文件、导出或克隆。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-405">Detailed reports are fully customizable and can be downloaded to a CSV file, exported, or cloned.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-406">有关这两个版本之间区别的完整说明，请参阅[本文](turning-on-and-using-call-quality-dashboard.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-406">For a full description of the difference between the two editions, see [this article](turning-on-and-using-call-quality-dashboard.md).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-407">2020年1月[的新增功能：下载 CQD 的 POWER BI 查询模板](https://github.com/MicrosoftDocs/OfficeDocs-SkypeForBusiness/blob/live/Teams/downloads/CQD-Power-BI-query-templates.zip?raw=true)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-407">New in January 2020: [Download Power BI query templates for CQD](https://github.com/MicrosoftDocs/OfficeDocs-SkypeForBusiness/blob/live/Teams/downloads/CQD-Power-BI-query-templates.zip?raw=true).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-408">可用于分析和报告 CQD 数据的自定义 Power BI 模板。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-408">Customizable Power BI templates you can use to analyze and report your CQD data.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-409">_图 4-CQD 报表类别_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-409">_Figure 4 - CQD report categories_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-410">汇总报表分为四个类别：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-410">The summary reports are divided into four categories:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-411">**摘要报告**重点介绍通过每天、每月和表报表分析质量趋势来帮助识别质量较差的子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-411">**Summary Reports** focus on analyzing quality trends with daily, monthly, and table reports to assist with identifying subnets that have poor quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-412">这是首次登录 CQD Online 时的默认登陆页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-412">This is the default landing page when you first sign in to CQD Online.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-413">**位置增强的报表**重点基于位置信息分析质量趋势。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-413">**Location-Enhanced Reports** focus on analyzing quality trends based on location information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-414">若要使用这些报表，您必须已上载了一个生成文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-414">To use these reports, you must have uploaded a building file.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-415">**可靠性报告**侧重于分析音频、视频、视频屏幕共享（VBSS）和应用共享的可靠性趋势。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-415">**Reliability Reports** focus on analyzing reliability trends for audio, video, video-based screen sharing (VBSS), and app sharing.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-416">**经验报告**是 "slimmed" 版本的详细 QER 模板，重点介绍了分析音频质量和可靠性的关键领域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-416">**Quality of Experience Reports** are a "slimmed-down" version of the detailed QER templates, focusing on key areas for analyzing audio quality and reliability.</span></span>

### <a name="report-types"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-417">报表类型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-417">Report types</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-418">你可以从 CQD 中的两种类型的报表中进行选择，具体取决于你希望查看数据的方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-418">You can choose from two types of reports in CQD, depending on how you want to view your data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-419">虽然本指南不介绍创建一种类型的报表的具体情况，但 QER CQD 模板提供了可自定义的图表和表报表的混合，供你使用：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-419">Although this guide doesn't cover the specifics of creating one type of report over another, the QER CQD templates provide a mix of customizable chart and table reports for you to use:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-420">图表报表创建以可视格式表示数据的图形条形图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-420">Chart reports create graphical bar charts to represent data in a visual format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-421">图表报表最适合用于在给定时间段内实现数据的可视化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-421">Chart reports are best used to visualize data over a given time period.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-422">当您将报表导出到 CSV 文件以便在 Microsoft Excel 中进行操作时，表格报表对于查看单个度量和维度非常有用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-422">Table reports are useful for looking at individual measurements and dimensions when you export the reports to CSV files for manipulation in Microsoft Excel.</span></span>

### <a name="tenant-id"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-423">租户 ID</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-423">Tenant ID</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-424">某些 CQD 报表要求你包含租户 ID 的筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-424">Some CQD reports require that you include a filter for your tenant ID.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-425">由于 CQD 聚合数据的方式，因此包含了联合参与者遥测。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-425">Due to the way CQD aggregates data, federated participant telemetry is included.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-426">尽管在分析趋势时这一点非常有用，但客户端和设备报表要求你将数据筛选到特定租户，以排除联合参与者遥测。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-426">Although this can prove valuable when analyzing trends, client and device reports require that you filter data to a specific tenant to exclude federated participant telemetry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-427">如果不知道租户 ID，可以使用以下方法之一来查找它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-427">If you don't know your tenant ID, you can use one of the following methods to find it.</span></span>

> [!Note]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-428">这些方法需要以下权限：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-428">These methods require the following permissions:</span></span><ul><li><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-429">全局管理员角色</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-429">Global Administrator Role</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-430">Skype for Business 管理员角色</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-430">Skype for Business Administrator Role</span></span></li></ul>

#### <a name="azure-portal"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-431">Azure 门户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-431">Azure portal</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-432">登录到 Microsoft Azure 门户：<https://portal.azure.com></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-432">Sign in to the Microsoft Azure portal: <https://portal.azure.com></span></span>

2.  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-433">选择 " **Azure Active Directory**"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-433">Select **Azure Active Directory**.</span></span>

3.  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-434">在 "**管理**" 下，选择 "**属性**"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-434">Under **Manage**, select **Properties**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-435">租户 ID 显示在 "**目录 id** " 框中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-435">The tenant ID is shown in the **Directory ID** box.</span></span>

#### <a name="azure-powershell"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-436">Azure PowerShell</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-436">Azure PowerShell</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-437">[安装 Microsoft Azure PowerShell 服务管理模块](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/azure/servicemanagement/install-azure-ps?view=azuresmps-4.0.0)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-437">[Install the Microsoft Azure PowerShell Service Management module](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/azure/servicemanagement/install-azure-ps?view=azuresmps-4.0.0).</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-438">出现提示时，打开 Azure PowerShell 命令窗口并运行以下脚本，输入 Office 365 凭据：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-438">Open an Azure PowerShell command window and run the following script, entering your Office 365 credentials when prompted:</span></span> 

   ```PowerShell
   Login-AzureRmAccount
   ```

3. <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-439">租户 ID 在输出中列出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-439">The tenant ID is listed in the output.</span></span>

#### <a name="skype-for-business-online-admin-center"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-440">Skype for Business Online 管理中心</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-440">Skype for Business Online Admin Center</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-441">转到 <https://portal.office.com>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-441">Go to <https://portal.office.com>.</span></span>

2.  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-442">通过租户管理员组织帐户登录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-442">Sign in with your tenant administrator organizational account.</span></span>

3.  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-443">选择 "**管理中心**" 下**的 "Skype for** business"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-443">Select **Skype for Business** under **Admin Centers**.</span></span>

4.  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-444">租户 ID 作为 "欢迎" 页面上的 "**组织 id** " 列出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-444">The tenant ID is listed as **Organization ID** on the Welcome page.</span></span>

#### <a name="skype-for-business-online-using-powershell"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-445">使用 PowerShell 的 Skype for Business Online</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-445">Skype for Business Online using PowerShell</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-446">[设置适用于 Windows PowerShell 的计算机](/SkypeForBusiness/set-up-your-computer-for-windows-powershell/set-up-your-computer-for-windows-powershell)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-446">[Set up your computer for Windows PowerShell](/SkypeForBusiness/set-up-your-computer-for-windows-powershell/set-up-your-computer-for-windows-powershell).</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-447">运行以下命令：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-447">Run the following command:</span></span>

   ```PowerShell
   (Get-cstenant).tenantid
   ```

3. <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-448">租户 ID 显示为 GUID。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-448">The tenant ID is displayed as a GUID.</span></span>

### <a name="teams-vs-skype-for-business"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-449">团队与 Skype for business</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-449">Teams vs. Skype for Business</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-450">CQD 可以报告团队和 Skype for business 遥测。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-450">CQD can report on both Teams and Skype for Business telemetry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-451">但是，有时你可能希望开发报表以查看与 Skype for Business 分开的团队遥测。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-451">However, there might be times when you want to develop a report to look at Teams telemetry separate from Skype for Business.</span></span>

#### <a name="summary-reports"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-452">摘要报告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-452">Summary reports</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-453">若要修改 "摘要报告" 页面以仅查看团队或 Skype for business，请从屏幕顶部选择 "**产品过滤器**" 下拉菜单，然后选择所需的产品。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-453">To modify the summary reports page to look at only Teams or Skype for Business, select the **Product Filter** drop-down menu from the top of the screen, and then select the product you want.</span></span>

#### <a name="detailed-reports"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-456">详细报告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-456">Detailed reports</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-457">若要筛选所有详细报表，请在浏览器栏中将以下内容追加到 URL 的末尾：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-457">To filter all detailed reports, in the browser bar, append the following to the end of the URL:</span></span>

```PowerShell
/filter/[AllStreams].[Is Teams]|[FALSE]
```

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-458">**上例**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-458">**Example:**</span></span>

```https://cqd.teams.microsoft.com/cqd/#/1234567/2018-5/filter/[AllStreams].[Is Teams]|[FALSE]```

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-459">有关 URL 筛选器的详细信息，请参阅本部分后面的[筛选报告](#filtering-reports)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-459">For more information about URL filters, see [Filtering reports](#filtering-reports) later in this section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-460">若要筛选单个详细报表，请将筛选``Is Teams``器添加到报表，并将其设置为 True 或 False。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-460">To filter an individual detailed report, add the filter ``Is Teams`` to the report and set it to True or False.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-461">有关详细信息，请参阅本部分后面的[编辑报告](#editing-reports)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-461">For more information, see [Editing reports](#editing-reports) later in this section.</span></span>

### <a name="managed-vs-unmanaged-networks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-464">托管网络与非托管网络</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-464">Managed vs. unmanaged networks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-465">默认情况下，CQD 中的所有终结点归为外部。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-465">By default, all endpoints in CQD are classified as external.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-466">一旦引入了生成文件，我们就可以开始查看托管终结点数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-466">As soon as a building file is introduced, we can begin to look at managed endpoint data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-467">正如前面所述，CQD 中的网络定义为：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-467">As previously discussed, networks in CQD are defined as:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-468">_托管网络_（通常称为内部或内部）可能受组织影响和控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-468">A _managed network_, often referred to as internal or inside, can be influenced and controlled by the organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-469">这包括内部 LAN、远程 WAN 和 VPN。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-469">This includes the internal LAN, the remote WAN, and VPN.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-470">_非托管网络_（通常称为外部网络或外部网络）不受组织影响或控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-470">An _unmanaged network_, often referred to as external or outside, can't be influenced or controlled by the organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-471">非托管网络的一个示例是旅馆或机场网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-471">An example of an unmanaged network is a hotel or airport network.</span></span>

### <a name="dimensions-measures-and-filters"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-472">维度、度量值和筛选器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-472">Dimensions, measures, and filters</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-473">标准格式的 CQD 查询包含以下所有三个参数：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-473">A well-formed CQD query contains all three of the following parameters:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-474">**维度：** 我希望如何对数据进行透视。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-474">**Dimension:** How I want to pivot on the data.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-475">**度量：** 我想要报告哪些内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-475">**Measure:** What I want to report on.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-476">**筛选器：** 我希望如何减少查询返回的数据集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-476">**Filter:** How I want to reduce the dataset the query returns.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-477">另一种查看方式是，_维度_是分组函数，_度量值_是我感兴趣的数据，_筛选器_是我希望将结果缩小到与 "我的查询" 相关的结果的方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-477">Another way to look at this is that a _dimension_ is the grouping function, a _measure_ is the data I'm interested in, and a _filter_ is how I want to narrow down the results to those that are relevant to my query.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-478">格式正确的查询示例**向我展示了 "子网 [维度] 的不良流 [Measure]"，用于构建 6 [Filter]**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-478">An example of a well-formed query is **Show me Poor Streams [Measure] by Subnet [Dimension] for Building 6 [Filter]**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-479">有关详细信息，请参阅[CQD 中可用的维度和度量](https://aka.ms/cqd-dm)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-479">For more information, see [Dimensions and measures available in CQD](https://aka.ms/cqd-dm).</span></span>

### <a name="first-vs-second"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-480">第一和第二</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-480">First vs. second</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-481">CQD 中的许多维度和度量值都属于第一或第二。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-481">Many of the dimensions and measures in CQD are classified as first or second.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-482">CQD 不使用 "调用方/被调用方" 字段-这些字段已被重命名 _，因为调用__方和被_调用方之间有介入的步骤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-482">CQD doesn't use caller/callee fields—these have been renamed _first_ and _second_ because there are intervening steps between the caller and callee.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-483">以下逻辑确定所涉及的终结点标记为 "第一个"：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-483">The following logic determines which endpoint involved is labeled as first:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-484">如果在流或呼叫中涉及服务器，则**首先**将始终是服务器终结点（会议服务器、中介服务器等）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-484">**First** will always be a server endpoint (Conference Server, Mediation Server, and so on) if a server is involved in the stream or call.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-485">**第二个**将始终是客户端终结点，除非该流位于两个服务器终结点之间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-485">**Second** will always be a client endpoint unless the stream is between two server endpoints.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-486">如果两个终结点的类型相同，则首先选择哪一个是基于用户代理类别的内部排序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-486">If both endpoints are the same type, the choice of which is first is based on internal ordering of the user agent category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-487">这样可以确保排序的一致性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-487">This ensures the ordering is consistent.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-488">有关在两个终结点相同时确定第一个或第二个终结点的详细信息，请参阅[CQD 中可用的维度和度量值](https://aka.ms/cqd-dm)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-488">For more information about determining the first or second endpoint when they're both the same, see [Dimensions and measures available in CQD](https://aka.ms/cqd-dm).</span></span>

### <a name="stream-vs-call"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-489">流与调用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-489">Stream vs. call</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-490">您需要了解通话和流之间的区别，以便正确选择要在 CQD 中查看的维度或度量值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-490">You need to understand the difference between a call and a stream to properly choose which dimensions or measures you'll be looking at in CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-491">尽管 CQD 的主要焦点位于流上，但也可以使用基于呼叫的度量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-491">Although CQD's primary focus is on streams, call-based measurements are also available.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-492">**流：**_流_存在于两个终结点之间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-492">**Stream:** A _stream_ exists between only two endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-493">每个方向只有一个流，并且需要两个流才能进行通信。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-493">There is only one stream for each direction, and two streams are required for communication.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-494">流对于调查建筑物、网络或子网很有用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-494">Streams are useful for investigating buildings, networks, or subnets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-495">在某些情况下，将在度量的名称中使用 call 和 stream （例如，呼叫设置流或呼叫中断流）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-495">In some cases, both call and stream are used in the measurement's name (for example, Call Setup Stream or Call Dropped Stream).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-496">这些仍属于流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-496">These are still classified as streams.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-497">**通话：**_通话_是来自所有参与者的所有流的分组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-497">**Call:** A _call_ is a grouping of all streams from all participants.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-498">通话至少包含两个流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-498">A call consists of—at minimum—two streams.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-499">单个调用将至少具有两个终结点，每个终结点至少有一个流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-499">A single call will have at least two endpoints, each with a minimum of one stream.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-500">有关维度或度量值是指调用还是流的其他指导，请参阅[CQD 中可用的维度和度量值](https://aka.ms/cqd-dm)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-500">For additional guidance on whether the dimension or measure is referring to a call or a stream, see [Dimensions and measures available in CQD](https://aka.ms/cqd-dm)</span></span>

### <a name="good-poor-and-unclassified-calls"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-501">良好、差和未分类的通话</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-501">Good, poor, and unclassified calls</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-502">通话被分类为 "良好"、"差" 或 "未分类"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-502">A call is categorized either as good, poor, or unclassified.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-503">让我们花一些时间来详细讨论每一种信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-503">Let's take a moment to talk about each one in more detail.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-504">**好或差：** 一个很好或很差的通话包括一个调用，其中包含一组完整的服务指标，由服务生成并接收完整的 QoE 报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-504">**Good or poor:** A good or poor call consists of a call that contains a complete set of service metrics, for which a full QoE report was generated and received by the service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-505">[在本指南前面部分中](#poor-stream-rate)，确定流是否正常或较差。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-505">Determining whether a stream is good or poor is described [earlier in this guide](#poor-stream-rate).</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-506">未**分类：** 未分类流不包含完整的一组服务指标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-506">**Unclassified:** An unclassified stream doesn't contain a full set of service metrics.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-507">这些调用可以是短时间，通常不会小于60秒-无法计算平均值，也不会生成 QoE 报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-507">These can be short calls—usually less than 60 seconds—where averages couldn't be computed and a QoE report wasn't generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-508">不受分类通话的最常见原因是几乎没有数据包利用率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-508">The most common reason for calls to be unclassified is that there was little to no packet utilization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-509">例如，参与者在静音中加入会议，而从不讲话。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-509">An example of this would be a participant who joins a meeting on mute and never speaks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-510">参与者正在接收，但无法传输媒体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-510">The participant is receiving, but not transmitting, media.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-511">如果没有传输媒体，则没有任何指标可供 CQD 用于分类终结点的出站媒体流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-511">Without media being transmitted, there won't be any metrics available for CQD to use to classify the endpoint's outbound media stream.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-512">有关流分类过程的详细信息，请参阅[本文](stream-classification-in-call-quality-dashboard.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-512">For more information about the stream classification process, see [this article](stream-classification-in-call-quality-dashboard.md).</span></span>

### <a name="common-subnets"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-513">常见子网</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-513">Common subnets</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-514">公用子网是由旅馆、家庭网络、热点和类似区域使用的专用子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-514">Common subnets are specific private subnets that are used by hotels, home networks, hotspots, and similar areas.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-515">由于这些子网的广泛使用，因此很难进行会审。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-515">These subnets are difficult to triage due to their widespread use.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-516">如果你的组织使用其中一个通用子网，我们建议你将该网络移动到另一个子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-516">If your organization uses one of these common subnets, we recommend that you move that network to another subnet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-517">这将使 CQD 中的报告更轻松。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-517">This will make reporting easier in CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-518">记下时，"所有网络" 模板中的报表已配置为排除这些子网，以将它们排除为质量较差的源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-518">When noted, reports in the All Networks template have been configured to exclude these subnets to eliminate them as a source of poor quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-519">常用子网定义如下。其影响将因组织而异。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-519">Common subnets are defined below; their impact will vary by organization.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-520">10.0.0.0/24</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-520">10.0.0.0/24</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-521">192.168.0.0/24</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-521">192.168.0.0/24</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-522">192.168.1.0/24</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-522">192.168.1.0/24</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-523">192.168.2.0/24</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-523">192.168.2.0/24</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-524">172.20.10.0/24</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-524">172.20.10.0/24</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-525">192.168.43.0/24</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-525">192.168.43.0/24</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-526">在调查使用公共子网的托管网络时，需要使用第二个反身本地 IP 维度来对子网进行分组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-526">When investigating a managed network that uses a common subnet, you'll need to use the Second Reflexive Local IP dimension to group subnets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-527">此维度包含终结点的公共 IP 地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-527">This dimension contains the endpoint's public IP address.</span></span>

## <a name="cqd-online"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-528">CQD Online</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-528">CQD Online</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-529">本部分介绍了访问 CQD 的基础知识。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-529">This section describes the fundamentals of accessing CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-530">指南适用于以下主题：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-530">Guidance is given for the following topics:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-531">联机访问 CQD</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-531">Accessing CQD online</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-532">CQD 入门</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-532">Getting started with CQD</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-533">在 CQD 中编辑报表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-533">Editing reports in CQD</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-534">在 CQD 中筛选报表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-534">Filtering reports in CQD</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-535">在 CQD 中导入报表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-535">Importing reports in CQD</span></span>

### <a name="getting-started"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-546">入门</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-546">Getting started</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-547">第一次浏览到 CQD 时，你将看到 "摘要报告" 页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-547">When you first browse to CQD, you'll see the Summary Reports page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-548">本指南中介绍的大部分报告都是自定义详细报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-548">Most of the reports described in this guide are custom detailed reports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-549">若要开始使用详细报表，请选择页面顶部的 "**摘要报表**"，然后选择 "**详细报表**"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-549">To get started using the detailed reports, select **Summary Reports** at the top of the page, and then choose **Detailed Reports**.</span></span>
