### <a name="editing-reports"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-566">编辑报表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-566">Editing reports</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-567">当您在报表的 "操作" 菜单上选择 "**编辑**" 时，将打开 "查询编辑器"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-567">When you select **Edit** on the action menu of a report, you'll open Query Editor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-568">每个报表都由 CQD 的查询支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-568">Each report is backed by a query to CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-569">报告是其查询返回的数据的可视化形式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-569">A report is a visualization of the data returned by its query.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-570">查询编辑器是除了报表的显示选项之外，还可用于编辑这些查询的 UI，如下图所示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-570">The Query Editor is a UI for editing these queries in addition to the display options for the report, as illustrated in the following figure.</span></span>

![显示组成正在编辑的报表的元素的屏幕截图。](media/qerguide-image-queryeditor.png)

|             |           |
| ------------|-----------|
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-572">![数字1的图标，引用上一个屏幕截图中的标注](media/qerguide-image-callout1.png "下列")</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-572">![Icon of the number 1, referencing a callout in the previous screenshot](media/qerguide-image-callout1.png "one")</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-573">从左窗格中选择维度、度量值和筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-573">You choose dimensions, measures, and filters from the left pane.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-574">指向现有值将显示 "关闭" 按钮（**X**），您可以选择删除该值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-574">Pointing to an existing value displays a close button (**X**) you can select to remove the value.</span></span><ul><li><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-575">通过选择维度或度量值，可以通过编辑 "**标题**" 字段来更改标题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-575">By selecting the dimension or measure, you can change the title by editing the **Title** field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-576">您也可以通过选择顶部窗格中的蓝色向上或向下箭头来更改顺序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-576">You can also change the order by selecting the blue Up or Down arrows in the top pane.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-577">选择标题**+** 旁边的 "（"）将打开用于添加新维度、度量值或筛选器的对话框。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-577">Selecting (**+**) next to a heading opens the dialog box for adding a new dimension, measure, or filter.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-578">在 "**查找**字段" 中输入维度、度量值或筛选器的前几个字母以筛选列表，以便更轻松地进行搜索。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-578">Enter the first few letters of the dimension, measure, or filter in the **Find a** field to filter the list for easier searching.</span></span></li></ul> |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-579">![数字2的图标，引用上一个屏幕截图中的标注](media/qerguide-image-callout2.png "双")</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-579">![Icon of the number 2, referencing a callout in the previous screenshot](media/qerguide-image-callout2.png "two")</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-580">顶部窗格显示图表自定义的选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-580">The top pane shows options for chart customization.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-581">![数字3的图标，引用上一个屏幕截图中的标注](media/qerguide-image-callout3.png "三个")</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-581">![Icon of the number 3, referencing a callout in the previous screenshot](media/qerguide-image-callout3.png "three")</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-582">查询编辑器显示报表的预览。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-582">The Query Editor shows a preview of the report.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-583">![数字4的图标，引用上一个屏幕截图中的标注](media/qerguide-image-callout4.png "共有")</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-583">![Icon of the number 4, referencing a callout in the previous screenshot](media/qerguide-image-callout4.png "four")</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-584">使用屏幕底部的**编辑**框创建或编辑报表的详细说明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-584">Use the **Edit** box at the bottom of the screen to create or edit a detailed description of the report.</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-585">_图 11-查询编辑器_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-585">_Figure 11 - Query Editor_</span></span>

### <a name="filtering-reports"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-586">筛选报表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-586">Filtering reports</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-587">所提供的模板包括几个内置查询和报表筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-587">The templates provided include several built-in queries and report filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-588">以下部分介绍了在整个模板中使用的最常见的筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-588">The following sections describe the most common filters used throughout the templates.</span></span>

#### <a name="url-filter"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-589">URL 筛选器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-589">URL filter</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-590">可以使用 URL 筛选器筛选特定维度的每个报表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-590">You can use a URL filter to filter every report for a specific dimension.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-591">最常见的 URL 筛选器用于筛选报表以排除联合参与者遥测，或专注于团队或 Skype for business Online。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-591">The most common URL filters are used to filter reports to exclude federated participant telemetry, or focus on Teams or Skype for Business Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-592">我们建议在使用筛选器时，为其添加书签以方便参考。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-592">We recommend that when using filters, you bookmark them for easy reference.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-593">当修正托管建筑物或网络（其中联合终结点可能会影响你的报表）时，从 CQD 报告中排除联合数据将非常有用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-593">Excluding federated data from CQD reports is useful when you're remediating managed buildings or networks where federated endpoints might influence your reports.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-594">若要实现 URL 筛选器，请在浏览器地址栏中将以下内容追加到 URL 的末尾：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-594">To implement a URL filter, in the browser address bar, append the following to the end of the URL:</span></span>

```PowerShell
/filter/[AllStreams].[Second Tenant Id]\|[YOUR TENANT ID HERE]
```

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-595">上例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-595">Example:</span></span>  

```https://cqd.teams.microsoft.com/cqd/#/1234567/2018-08/filter/[AllStreams].[Second Tenant Id]|[TENANTID]```

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-596">若要筛选团队或 Skype for business 的报表，请将以下内容附加到 URL 的末尾：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-596">To filter the reports for Teams or Skype for Business, append the following to the end of the URL:</span></span>

```PowerShell
/filter/[AllStreams].[Is Teams]|[TRUE | FALSE]
```

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-597">上例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-597">Example:</span></span>

```https://cqd.teams.microsoft.com/cqd/#/1234567/2018-08/filter/[AllStreams].[Is Teams]|[TRUE]```


> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-598">上面的 URL 示例仅适用于视觉表示形式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-598">The URL examples above are for visual representation only.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-599">请使用的默认 CQD 链接<https://cqd.teams.microsoft.com>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-599">Please use the default CQD link of <https://cqd.teams.microsoft.com>.</span></span>


#### <a name="query-filters"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-600">查询筛选器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-600">Query filters</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-601">查询筛选器通过在 CQD 中使用查询编辑器实现。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-601">Query filters are implemented by using the Query Editor in CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-602">这些筛选器用于减少 CQD 返回的记录数，从而最大程度减少报表的总体大小和查询时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-602">These filters are used to reduce the number of records returned by CQD, thus minimizing the report's overall size and query times.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-603">这对于筛选出非托管网络尤其有用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-603">This is especially useful for filtering out unmanaged networks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-604">下表中列出的筛选器使用正则表达式（RegEx）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-604">The filters listed in the following table use regular expressions (RegEx).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-605">_表 3-查询筛选器_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-605">_Table 3 - Query filters_</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-606">筛选器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-606">Filter</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-607">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-607">Description</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-608">CQD 查询筛选器示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-608">CQD query filter example</span></span>      |
|----------------|----------------------|-------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-609">无空值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-609">No blank values</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-610">某些筛选器没有用于筛选空值的选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-610">Some filters don't have the option to filter for blank values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-611">若要手动筛选空值，请使用空白表达式，并将筛选器设置为等于或不等于，具体取决于你的需求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-611">To filter blank values manually, use the blank expression and set the filter to Equals or Not Equals, depending on your needs.</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-612">第二建筑物\< \> \^ \\名称 s\*\$</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-612">Second Building Name \<\> \^\\s\*\$</span></span>                       |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-613">排除公共子网</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-613">Exclude common subnets</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-614">如果没有有效的生成文件以从非托管网络单独托管，则报告中将包含家庭网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-614">Without a valid building file to separate managed from unmanaged networks, home networks will be included in the reports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-615">这些主子网位于其控制范围之外，可以从报表中快速排除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-615">These home subnets are outside the scope of IT's control and can be quickly excluded from a report.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-616">本指南中定义的常用子网是10.0.0.0、192.168.1.0 和192.168.0.0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-616">Common subnets, as defined in this guide, are 10.0.0.0, 192.168.1.0 and 192.168.0.0.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-617">第二\< \>子\|网\| 10.0.0.0 192.168.0.0 192.168.1。0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-617">Second Subnet \<\> 10.0.0.0 \| 192.168.0.0 \| 192.168.1.0</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-618">仅限内部查看</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-618">View inside only</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-619">用于筛选托管（内部）或非托管（外部）的报表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-619">Used to filter a report for managed (inside) or unmanaged (outside).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-620">托管 CQD 模板已预配置了这些筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-620">The managed CQD template is already preconfigured with these filters.</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-621">第二内部公司内部公司 = 内部</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-621">Second Inside Corp = Inside</span></span>        |

#### <a name="report-filters"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-622">报表筛选器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-622">Report filters</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-623">报表筛选器通过在 "查询编辑器" 或直接添加到报表中向呈现的报表添加筛选器来实现。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-623">Report filters are implemented by adding a filter to the rendered report either in the Query Editor or directly to the report.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-624">在整个模板中使用以下报表筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-624">The following report filters are used throughout the template.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-625">_表 4-报表筛选器_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-625">_Table 4 - Report filters_</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-626">筛选器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-626">Filter</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-627">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-627">Description</span></span>                            | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-628">CQD 报表筛选器示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-628">CQD report filter example</span></span>         |

| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-629">Month</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-629">Month</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-630">首先从年开始，然后是 "月"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-630">Start with the year first, then month.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-631">2017-10</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-631">2017-10</span></span>                           |

## <a name="import-the-cqd-templates"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-641">导入 CQD 模板</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-641">Import the CQD templates</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-642">本指南包含[两个特选 CQD 模板](https://aka.ms/qertemplates)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-642">This guide includes [two curated CQD templates](https://aka.ms/qertemplates).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-643">这些模板提高了 CQD 的使用，并为您提供了快速利用 CQD 功能来对用户的团队或 Skype for business 体验产生影响的机会。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-643">These templates accelerate your usage of CQD and provide you an opportunity to quickly leverage CQD's capabilities to make an impact on your users' Teams or Skype for Business experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-644">"所有网络" 模板（虽然已优化为使用生成数据文件）可用于在 CQD 中收集和上载构建信息，如下一节中所述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-644">The All Networks template, though optimized to work with a building data file, can be used while you work toward collecting and uploading building information into CQD, as described in the next section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-645">**若要导入模板（。CQDX）进入 CQD Online**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-645">**To import the templates (.CQDX) into CQD Online**</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-646">转到 <https://cqd.teams.microsoft.com>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-646">Go to <https://cqd.teams.microsoft.com>.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-647">使用 Office 365 管理凭据进行身份验证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-647">Authenticate by using your Office 365 Administrative credentials.</span></span>

   > [!NOTE]
   > <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-648">您必须具有全局管理员、Skype for business 管理员或报表读者角色才能访问 CQD。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-648">You must have the Global Administrator, Skype for Business Administrator, or Report Readers role to access CQD.</span></span> 

3. <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-649">选择页面顶部的 "**摘要报告**" 菜单，然后选择 "**详细报告**"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-649">Select the **Summary Reports** menu at the top of the page, and then choose **Detailed Reports**.</span></span>

4. <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-650">在 "摘要" 窗格中，选择 "**导入**"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-650">On the summary pane, select **Import**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-651">转到 CQDX 保存的位置，选择 CQDX 模板，然后选择 "**打开**"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-651">Go to the CQDX saved location, select the CQDX template, and then select **Open**.</span></span>

5. <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-652">上载模板后，将显示一个弹出窗口，显示 "报表导入成功" 消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-652">After the template is uploaded, a pop-up window will display the message "Report import was successful."</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-653">选择 **"确定"。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-653">Select **OK.**</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-654">![成功导入通知的屏幕截图](media/qerguide-image-importmessage.png "已成功导入模板的通知")</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-654">![Screenshot of successful import notification](media/qerguide-image-importmessage.png "Notification that the template was successfully imported")</span></span>

6. <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-655">对第二个 CQD 模板重复步骤4和步骤5。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-655">Repeat steps 4 and 5 for the second CQD template.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-656">CQD 模板按用户导入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-656">The CQD templates are imported per user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-657">如果其他用户需要使用该报表，他们必须登录并将模板导入其 CQD 实例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-657">If additional users need to use the report, they must sign in and import the templates into their CQD instance.</span></span> 


## <a name="building-mapping"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-658">构建映射</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-658">Building mapping</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-659">在团队或 Skype for business Online 部署中，所有客户端都是外部客户端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-659">In a Teams or Skype for Business Online deployment, all clients are external.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-660">也就是说，默认情况下，所有客户端都在 CQD Online 中报告为外部，无论客户端是否连接到内部公司网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-660">That has the implication that by default, all clients are reported as outside in CQD Online, regardless of whether the client was connected on an internal corporate network.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-661">在使用 CQD 时，你需要知道终结点的位置以及它是否已连接到你可以管理的网络或无法管理的网络（假定你只能改进可管理的网络）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-661">When you work with CQD, you need to know the location of an endpoint and whether it was connected to a network you can manage or a network you can't manage—the assumption being that you can only improve networks you can manage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-662">通过将子网和生成信息上载到 CQD Online，你可以启用 CQD 以确定终结点是否已连接到内部公司/托管网络或外部/非托管网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-662">By uploading subnet and building information to CQD Online, you enable CQD to determine whether the endpoint was connected to an internal corporate/managed network or to an external/unmanaged network.</span></span>

### <a name="building-data-file-structure"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-663">构建数据文件结构</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-663">Building data file structure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-664">你上载的数据文件的格式必须满足以下要求才能在上载之前通过验证检查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-664">The format of the data file you upload must meet the following requirements to pass the validation check before uploading.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-665">文件必须是 TSV 文件，这意味着对于每一行，每一列都由制表符分隔，或 CSV 文件，其中每列由逗号分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-665">The file must be either a TSV file—which means that for each row, each column is separated by a Tab character—or a CSV file in which each column is separated by a comma.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-666">文件不能大于 50 MB。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-666">The file can't be larger than 50 MB.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-667">数据文件的内容*不能包含表格标题*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-667">The content of the data file *must not include table headers*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-668">换句话说，数据文件的第一行必须是实际数据，而不是列标题（如 "Network"）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-668">In other words, the first line of the data file must be real data, not column headings such as "Network."</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-669">对于每个列，数据类型只能是 String、Number 或 Bool。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-669">For each column, the data type can only be String, Number, or Bool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-670">如果数据类型为 "数字"，则值必须为数值;如果是 Bool，则该值必须是0或1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-670">If the data type is Number, the value must be a numeric value; if it's Bool, the value must be either 0 or 1.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-671">对于每一列，如果数据类型为 String，则数据可以为空（但必须用适当的分隔符（即制表符或逗号）分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-671">For each column, if the data type is String, the data can be empty (but still must be separated by an appropriate delimiter—that is, a Tab character or comma).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-672">这只是将该字段分配为空字符串值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-672">This just assigns that field an empty string value.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-673">每一行必须有14列（如果要添加可选的 VPN 列，则为15）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-673">There must be 14 columns for each row (or 15 if you want to add the optional VPN column).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-674">每列必须具有下表中所述的数据类型，并且列必须按照表中列出的顺序排列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-674">Each column must have the data type described in the following table, and the columns must be in the order listed in the table.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-675">_表 5-构建文件结构_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-675">_Table 5 - Building file structure_</span></span>

#### <a name="supernetting"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-741">Supernetting</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-741">Supernetting</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-742">你可以使用 supernetting （通常称为无类别的域间路由（CIDR））来代替定义每个子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-742">You can use supernetting, commonly called Classless Inter-Domain Routing (CIDR,) in place of defining each subnet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-743">*Supernet*是共享单个路由前缀的若干子网的组合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-743">A *supernet* is a combination of several subnets that share a single routing prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-744">你可以使用 supernetted 地址，而不是为每个子网添加条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-744">Instead of adding an entry for each subnet, you can use the supernetted address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-745">支持 Supernetting，但我们不建议使用它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-745">Supernetting is supported, but we don't recommend using it.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-746">例如，Contoso 的市场营销大楼由以下子网组成：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-746">For example, Contoso's marketing building is made up of the subnets below:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-747">10.1.0.0/24-第一层</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-747">10.1.0.0/24—first floor</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-748">10.1.1.0/24-第二层</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-748">10.1.1.0/24—second floor</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-749">10.1.2.0/24-第三个楼层</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-749">10.1.2.0/24—third floor</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-750">10.1.3.0/24-第四个楼层</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-750">10.1.3.0/24—fourth floor</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-751">你可以使用 supernetted 地址（在本例中为 10.1.0.0/22），而不是为每个子网添加条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-751">Instead of adding an entry for each subnet, you can use the supernetted address—in this example, 10.1.0.0/22.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-752">Network = 10.1.0。0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-752">Network = 10.1.0.0</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-753">网络范围 = 22</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-753">Network Range = 22</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-754">在实现 supernetting 之前，需要考虑以下几点：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-754">Here are a few things to consider before you implement supernetting:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-755">Supernetting 只能在具有8位到28位掩码的子网映射中使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-755">Supernetting can only be used in a subnet mapping with 8-bit to 28-bit mask.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-756">Supernetting 花费的时间更少，但它以减少数据丰富的成本为代价。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-756">Supernetting takes less time up front, but it comes at the cost of reducing the richness of your data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-757">假设存在涉及子网200.1.2.0 的质量问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-757">Let's say there's a quality problem involving subnet 200.1.2.0.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-758">如果你已实现 supernetting，你将不知道子网所在的位置或网络的类型（例如，实验）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-758">If you implemented supernetting, you won't know where in the building the subnet is located or what type of network it is (for example, a lab).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-759">如果您已为建筑物和上传的地板位置信息定义了所有子网，您将能够看到这种区别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-759">If you'd defined all the subnets for a building and uploaded floor location information, you'd be able to see that distinction.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-760">请务必确保 supernetted 地址正确，并且不会捕获不需要的子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-760">It's important to ensure that the supernetted address is correct and isn't catching unwanted subnets.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-761">在数据中查找192.168.0.0 非常常见。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-761">It's quite common to find 192.168.0.0 in data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-762">对于许多组织，这表示用户在家中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-762">For many organizations, this indicates that the user is at home.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-763">对于其他人，这是卫星办公室的 IP 地址方案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-763">For others, this is the IP address scheme for a satellite office.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-764">如果你的组织具有使用此配置的办事处，则不要将其包含在你的构建文件中，因为很难通过使用公共子网来区分家庭网络和内部网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-764">If your organization does have offices that use this configuration, don't include it in your building file because it's difficult to distinguish between home and internal networks by using common subnets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-765">请参阅本指南前面部分的有关[公用子网](#common-subnets)的部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-765">See the section about [common subnets](#common-subnets), earlier in this guide.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-766">网络范围可用于表示 supernet。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-766">The network range can be used to represent a supernet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-767">将检查所有新生成数据文件上是否有任何重叠区域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-767">All new building data file uploads will be checked for any overlapping ranges.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-768">如果你以前上载了一个生成文件，你应该下载当前文件并再次上载它以识别任何重叠并解决问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-768">If you've previously uploaded a building file, you should download the current file and upload it again to identify any overlaps and fix the issue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-769">以前上载的文件中的任何重叠都可能会导致向报表中的建筑物进行错误的子网映射。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-769">Any overlap in previously uploaded files might result in the wrong mappings of subnets to buildings in the reports.</span></span>

#### <a name="vpn"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-770">VPN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-770">VPN</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-771">客户端发送到 Office 365 的体验质量（QoE）数据（CQD 数据来源的位置）包括 VPN 标志。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-771">The quality of experience (QoE) data that clients send to Office 365—which is where CQD data is sourced from—includes a VPN flag.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-772">CQD 将看到这是第一个 VPN 和第二个 VPN 维度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-772">CQD will see this as the First VPN and Second VPN dimensions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-773">但是，此标志依赖于 VPN 供应商向 Windows 报告，VPN 网络适配器已注册为远程访问适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-773">However, this flag relies on VPN vendors' reporting to Windows that the VPN network adapter registered is a Remote Access adapter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-774">并非所有 VPN 供应商都正确注册远程访问适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-774">Not all VPN vendors properly register Remote Access adapters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-775">因此，你可能无法使用内置的 VPN 查询筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-775">Because of this, you might not be able to use the built-in VPN query filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-776">可通过两种方法在构建信息文件中容纳 VPN 子网：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-776">There are two approaches to accommodating VPN subnets in the building information file:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-777">使用 VPN 子网的此字段中的文本 "VPN" 定义**网络名称**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-777">Define a **Network Name** by using the text "VPN" in this field for VPN subnets.</span></span>

  ![使用网络名称显示 VPN 的 QCD 报告屏幕截图](media/qerguide-image-vpnnetworkname.png)

  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-779">_图 12-使用网络名称的 VPN_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-779">_Figure 12 - VPN using network name_</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-780">使用 VPN 子网的此字段中的文本 "VPN" 定义**建筑物名称**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-780">Define a **Building Name** by using the text "VPN" in this field for VPN subnets.</span></span>

  ![显示使用建筑物名称的 VPN 的 QCD 报告屏幕截图](media/qerguide-image-vpnbuildingname.png)

  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-782">_图 13-使用建筑物名称的 VPN_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-782">_Figure 13 - VPN using building name_</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-783">某些 VPN 实现不会准确报告子网信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-783">Certain VPN implementations don't accurately report subnet information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-784">这是因为有一个32位子网提供了 VPN 客户端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-784">This is because the VPN client is provided with a 32-bit subnet.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-785">正如上一节中所述，CQD 无法正确识别32位子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-785">As mentioned in the previous section, CQD is unable to properly identify a 32-bit subnet.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-786">若要在 CQD 中准确地标识 VPN 子网，请在生成文件中将 VPN 字段设置为1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-786">To accurately identify a VPN subnet in CQD set the VPN field to 1 in the building file.</span></span>


> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-787">当基础互联网连接为无线时，misidentify 将网络连接称为有线的 VPN 连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-787">VPN connections have been known to misidentify the network connection as wired when the underlying internet connection is wireless.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-788">在通过 VPN 连接查看高质量时，无法假定已准确识别连接类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-788">When looking at quality over VPN connections, you can't assume that the connection type has been accurately identified.</span></span>

### <a name="uploading-building-information"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-789">上载建筑物信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-789">Uploading building information</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-790">CQD 摘要报告仪表板包括**租户数据上载**页面，该页面通过选择右上角中的**租户数据上载**链接标记进行访问（查找齿轮图标）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-790">The CQD Summary Reports dashboard includes a **Tenant Data Upload** page, accessed by selecting the **Tenant Data Upload** link tag in the upper-right corner (look for the gear icon).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-791">此页面用于管理员上载其自己的信息，例如 IP 地址和地理信息的映射、映射每个无线访问点及其 MAC 地址等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-791">This page is used for admins to upload their own information, such as mapping of IP address and geographical information, mapping each wireless access point and its MAC address, and so on.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-792">通过浏览转到 CQD Online <https://cqd.teams.microsoft.com>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-792">Go to CQD Online by browsing to <https://cqd.teams.microsoft.com>.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-793">选择右上角的齿轮图标，然后从 "**摘要报告**" 页面中选择 "**租户数据上载**"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-793">Select the gear icon in the upper-right corner, and choose **Tenant Data Upload** from the **Summary Reports** page.</span></span>

   ![在上载数据时出现的对话框的屏幕截图](media/qerguide-image-tenantdataupload.png)

   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-795">_图 14-租户数据上载菜单_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-795">_Figure 14 - Tenant Data Upload menu_</span></span>

3. <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-796">或者，如果你首次访问 CQD，系统将要求你上载数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-796">Alternatively, if this is your first time visiting CQD, you'll be asked to upload building data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-797">你可以选择 "**立即上载**" 以快速导航到**租户数据上载**页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-797">You can select **Upload Now** to quickly navigate to the **Tenant Data Upload** page.</span></span>

   ![通知用户上载生成数据的横幅的屏幕截图](media/qerguide-image-buildingdatauploadbanner.png)

   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-799">_图 15-构建数据上载横幅_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-799">_Figure 15 - Building data upload banner_</span></span>

4. <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-800">在 "**租户数据上载**" 页面上，选择 "**浏览**" 以选择数据文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-800">On the **Tenant Data Upload** page, select **Browse** to choose a data file.</span></span>

5. <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-801">选择数据文件后，指定 "**开始日期**"，（可选）指定结束日期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-801">After selecting a data file, specify **Start date** and, optionally, specify an end date.</span></span>

6. <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-802">选择 "**开始日期**" 后，选择 "**上传**" 将文件上传到 CQD。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-802">After selecting **Start date**, select **Upload** to upload the file to CQD.</span></span> <br><br><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-803">在上载文件之前，它将经过验证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-803">Before the file is uploaded, it's validated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-804">如果验证失败，则会显示一条错误消息，要求你更正该文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-804">If validation fails, an error message is displayed requesting that you correct the file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-805">下图显示了当数据文件中的列数不正确时出现的错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-805">The following figure shows an error occurring when the number of columns in the data file is incorrect.</span></span>

   ![显示生成数据上载错误的对话框示例](media/qerguide-image-buildingdatauploaderror.png)
 
   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-807">_图 16-生成数据上载错误_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-807">_Figure 16 - Building data upload error_</span></span>

7. <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-808">如果验证期间没有出现错误，文件上载将成功。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-808">If no errors occur during validation, the file upload will succeed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-809">然后，你可以在 "我的上**传**" 表中看到上载的数据文件，其中显示了当前租户在该页面底部的所有上载文件的完整列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-809">You can then see the uploaded data file in the **My uploads** table, which shows the full list of all uploaded files for the current tenant at the bottom of that page.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-810">最多可能需要四个小时才能完成处理生成文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-810">It can take up to four hours to finish processing the building file.</span></span> <br><br> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-811">如果你已经上载了一个生成文件，但需要添加可能已错过或排除的子网，请通过添加新的子网、删除当前文件并重新上载新编辑的文件来修改原始文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-811">If you've already uploaded a building file and need to add subnets that might have been missed or excluded, modify the original file by adding the new subnets, remove the current file, and re-upload the newly edited file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-812">CQD 中只能有一个活动的构建数据文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-812">There can be only one active building data file in CQD.</span></span> 


### <a name="updating-a-building-file"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-813">更新生成文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-813">Updating a building file</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-814">在收集生成和子网信息时，管理员通常会在一段时间内将生成文件上载到多个迭代中，并在新子网可用时添加新的子网和生成信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-814">While gathering building and subnet information, administrators will often upload the building file in multiple iterations over time, adding new subnets and their building information as it becomes available.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-815">出现这种情况时，你需要重新上载你的构建文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-815">When this occurs, you'll need to re-upload your building file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-816">此过程类似于上一节中所述的初始上载，还有一些例外，如下部分所述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-816">This process is like the initial upload as described in the previous section, with a few exceptions as noted in the following section.</span></span>

> [!Important]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-817">一次只能有一个生成文件处于活动状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-817">Only one building file can be active at a time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-818">多个生成文件不具有累积性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-818">Multiple building files aren't cumulative.</span></span>

#### <a name="adding-net-new-subnets"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-819">添加全新的子网</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-819">Adding net new subnets</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-820">有时，你需要将新的子网添加到 CQD 中的子网，而不是你的网络拓扑的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-820">There are times when you'll need to add net new subnets to CQD that weren't originally part of your network topology.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-821">若要添加全新的子网，请在 CQD 租户数据上载门户中执行以下操作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-821">To add net new subnets, do the following in the CQD Tenant Data Upload portal:</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-822">编辑原始构建文件，并提供在获取网络新子网之前至少一天出现的结束日期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-822">Edit the original building file and provide an end date that occurs at least one day before the net new subnets were acquired.</span></span>
2.  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-823">如果尚未有最新的副本，请下载原始文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-823">Download the original file, if you don't already have an up-to-date copy.</span></span>
3.  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-824">将新的全新子网附加到原始生成文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-824">Append the net new subnets to the original building file.</span></span>
4.  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-825">按照上述相同过程上载新修改的生成文件，并将开始日期设置为上一个生成文件结束后的一天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-825">Upload the newly modified building file following the same process as above, and set the start date for one day after the previous building file ends.</span></span>

#### <a name="updating-the-current-building-file"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-826">更新当前构建文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-826">Updating the current building file</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-827">如果生成文件已上载，但需要添加缺少的子网，请在 CQD 租户数据上载门户中执行以下操作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-827">If a building file is already uploaded but you need to add missing subnets, do the following in the CQD Tenant Data Upload portal:</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-828">如果尚未有最新的副本，请下载原始文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-828">Download the original file, if you don't already have an up-to-date copy.</span></span>
2.  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-829">删除 CQD 中的当前文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-829">Remove the current file in CQD.</span></span>
3.  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-830">将新子网追加到原始文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-830">Append the new subnets to the original file.</span></span>
4.  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-831">上载构建文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-831">Upload the building file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-832">请务必先将开始日期设置为至少八个月，这样 CQD 将处理历史记录数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-832">Be sure to set the start date to at least eight months prior so that CQD will process historical data.</span></span>

### <a name="missing-subnets"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-833">缺少子网</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-833">Missing subnets</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-834">在上载托管网络的生成信息后，每个托管网络都应具有一个建筑物关联。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-834">After you upload building information for managed networks, every managed network should have a building association.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-835">但是，这并不总是这样。通常，缺少几个子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-835">However, this won't always be the case; typically, a few subnets are missed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-836">本部分介绍如何验证缺少的网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-836">This section covers how to validate those missing networks.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-837">浏览到 CQD Online 中的**详细报告**页面，并导航到 CQD 模板中包含的**缺失子网报告**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-837">Browse to the **Detailed Reports** page in CQD Online and navigate to the **Missing Subnet Report** included in the CQD templates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-838">这将显示包含10个或更多音频流的所有子网，这些流在建筑物数据文件中未定义且标记为外部。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-838">This presents all the subnets with 10 or more audio streams that aren't defined in the building data file and are being marked as outside.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-839">确保此列表中没有托管网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-839">Ensure that there are no managed networks in this list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-840">如果缺少子网，请更新原始生成数据文件，然后将其重新上载到 CQD。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-840">If subnets are missing, update the original building data file and re-upload it to CQD.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-841">你需要将租户 ID 作为**第二租户 id**的查询筛选器添加到此报表，以筛选报表以仅查看你的组织的租户数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-841">You'll need to add your tenant ID as a query filter for **Second Tenant ID** to this report to filter the report to view only your organization's tenant data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-842">否则，报表将显示联合子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-842">Otherwise, the report will show federated subnets.</span></span>

> [!NOTE] 
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-843">请确保将 "月" 报表筛选器调整为当前月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-843">Be sure to adjust the Month Year report filter to the current month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-844">选择 "**编辑**"，然后调整 "**月**" 报表筛选器以保存新的默认月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-844">Select **Edit**, and adjust the **Month Year** report filter to save the new default month.</span></span>

![显示丢失的子网报表的屏幕截图](media/qerguide-image-missingbuildingreport.png)

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-846">_图 17-缺少生成报告_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-846">_Figure 17 - Missing Building Report_</span></span>

### <a name="building-mapping-tools"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-847">构建地图工具</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-847">Building mapping tools</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-848">让我们面对 it，可能很难在你的组织中映射子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-848">Let's face it, mapping out subnets in your organization can be difficult.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-849">较大的全局网络非常复杂，有不同的团队管理各自的区域，并且网络拓扑可能没有单一来源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-849">Large global networks are very complex, with different teams managing their respective regions, and there might be no single source of truth for the network topology.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-850">有两个工具可用于帮助开始建筑物映射练习，如以下部分所述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-850">There are two tools available to assist with starting the building mapping exercise, described in the following sections.</span></span>

#### <a name="cqd-tools"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-851">CQD 工具</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-851">CQD tools</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-852">这些工具基于 PowerShell，并且可以利用 Active Directory （AD）站点和服务以及 Microsoft DHCP 服务来帮助预填充你的构建文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-852">These tools are based on PowerShell and can leverage Active Directory (AD) Sites and Services and Microsoft DHCP services to help pre-populate your building file.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-853">这些工具将帮助你执行以下任务：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-853">These tools will help with the following tasks:</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-854">查询广告网站和服务，并基于其中包含的信息创建构建文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-854">Query AD Sites and Services, and create a building file based on the information contained within.</span></span>
2.  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-855">查询 Microsoft DHCP 服务器或服务器以提取子网信息并自动创建构建文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-855">Query a Microsoft DHCP server or servers to pull subnet information and automatically create a building file.</span></span>
3.  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-856">验证现有生成文件、检查重复项和重叠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-856">Validate an existing building file, checking for duplicates and overlaps.</span></span>
4.  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-857">在 CQD 中查找未映射的子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-857">Find unmapped subnets in CQD.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-858">有关此工具的详细信息，请参阅[此博客文章](https://aka.ms/cqdtools)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-858">For more information about this tool, see [this blog post](https://aka.ms/cqdtools).</span></span>

#### <a name="network-planner"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-859">Network Planner</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-859">Network Planner</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-860">网络规划器只需几个简单的步骤即可确定和组织你的云语音部署的网络要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-860">The Network Planner determines and organizes your network requirements for your Cloud Voice deployment in just a few simple steps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-861">通过提供你的组织的网络详细信息和云语音使用，你可以大致计算云语音部署的网络要求、管理和导出这些详细信息以进行报告，以及查看用于进一步调查的区域以及后续步骤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-861">By providing your organization's networking details and Cloud Voice usage, you can get an approximate calculation of the network requirements for your Cloud Voice deployment, manage and export these details for reporting, and view areas for further investigation and next steps.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-862">虽然网络规划器不会完全自动自动生成映射过程，但在将网络信息输入网络 Planner 后，可以将其导出到准备上载的构建文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-862">Although the Network Planner doesn't automate the building mapping process entirely, after network information is entered into the Network Planner it can then be exported to a building file ready for upload.</span></span>

## <a name="reliability-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-863">可靠性调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-863">Reliability investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-864">提高质量的第一步是评估整个组织的可靠性状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-864">The first step to improving quality is to assess the state of reliability across the organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-865">由于可靠性对于积极的用户体验至关重要，因此我们从衡量可靠性的两个组件开始：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-865">Because reliability is vital to a positive user experience, we start with the two components that measure reliability:</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-866">**设置失败：** 无法建立通话。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-866">**Setup failures:** The call couldn't be established.</span></span>

2.  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-867">**删除失败：** 通话已建立且意外终止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-867">**Drop failures:** The call was established and unexpectedly terminated.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-868">在本部分中，我们将介绍用于调查两个区域的方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-868">Throughout this section, we'll cover methods to investigate both areas.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-869">本指南不介绍这些模板中包含的所有报表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-869">Not all reports included in the templates are covered in this guide.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-870">但是，下面介绍的调查方法仍适用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-870">However, the methods of investigation explained below still apply.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-871">有关详细信息，请参阅各个报告说明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-871">Please refer to the individual report description for more information.</span></span>


### <a name="setup-failures"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-872">设置失败</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-872">Setup failures</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-873">首先优先考虑此区域中的修正设置失败，因为这些失败会对用户体验产生严重的负面影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-873">Prioritize remediating setup failures in this area first, because these failures have a significant negative impact on the user experience.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-874">通过评估组织的整体设置故障百分比来开始调查，然后根据构建或网络的最高百分比确定调查范围。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-874">Begin your investigation by assessing the percentage of overall setup failures for the organization, and then prioritize areas of investigation based on the highest percentage by building or network.</span></span> 

#### <a name="setup-failure-trend-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-875">设置故障趋势分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-875">Setup failure trend analysis</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-876">此报告显示流、流设置失败和流设置失败率的总数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-876">This report displays the total amount of streams, stream setup failures, and the stream setup failure rate.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-877">指向任意一个列以显示其单个值，如下图所示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-877">Point to any one of the columns to display its individual values, as shown in the following figure.</span></span>

##### <a name="analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-880">定量分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-880">Analysis</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-881">通过使用此报表，你可以回答以下问题并确定下一个操作过程：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-881">By using this report, you can answer the following questions and determine your next course of action:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-882">当前月份的通话设置总失败百分比是多少？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-882">What is the total call setup failure percentage for the current month?</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-883">是否已定义的目标度量值低于或高于其总呼叫设置失败百分比？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-883">Is the total call setup failure percentage below or above the defined target metric?</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-884">故障趋势是否比上个月更糟或更好？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-884">Is the failure trend worse or better than the previous month?</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-885">故障趋势是增长、稳定还是降低？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-885">Is the failure trend increasing, steady, or decreasing?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-886">无论以前的答案如何，都可以通过使用辅助子报表查找可能需要修正的任何单个建筑物或子网来进一步调查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-886">Irrespective of the previous answers, take the time to investigate further by using the companion sub-reports to look for any individual buildings or subnets that might need remediation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-887">尽管整体失败率可能低于目标度量值，但一个或多个建筑物或网络的故障率可能高于目标指标，需要调查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-887">Although the overall failure rate might be below the target metric, the failure rates for one or more buildings or networks might be above the target metric and need investigation.</span></span>

#### <a name="setup-failure-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-888">设置失败调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-888">Setup failure investigations</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-889">此摘要报告用于发现和隔离任何可能需要补救的建筑物或网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-889">This summary report is used to discover and isolate any buildings or networks that might need remediation.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-890">请确保将 "月" 报表筛选器调整为当前月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-890">Be sure to adjust the Month Year report filter to the current month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-891">选择 "**编辑**"，然后调整 "**月**" 报表筛选器以保存新的默认月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-891">Select **Edit**, and adjust the **Month Year** report filter to save the new default month.</span></span>


![显示设置失败的屏幕截图](media/qerguide-image-setupfailuresbysubnet.png)

##### <a name="remediation"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-894">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-894">Remediation</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-895">专注于具有最大故障量的建筑物或子网上的第一项补救措施。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-895">Focus your first remediation efforts on buildings or subnets that have the largest volume of failures.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-896">这将最大程度地提高用户体验的影响，并有助于快速降低组织呼叫设置失败的速率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-896">This will maximize impact on the user experience and help to quickly reduce the rate of organizational call setup failures.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-897">下表列出了由 CQD 报告的安装失败的两个原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-897">The following table lists the two reasons for setup failures as reported by CQD.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-898">_表 7-呼叫设置失败的原因_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-898">_Table 7 – Reasons for Call Setup Failures_</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-899">呼叫设置失败原因</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-899">Call Setup Failures reason</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-900">典型原因</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-900">Typical cause</span></span>                    |
|----------------------------------|----------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-901">缺少固件深层数据包检查例外规则</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-901">Missing FW Deep Packet Inspection Exemption Rule</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-902">指示由于深入的数据包检查规则，沿路径的网络设备阻止媒体路径被建立。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-902">Indicates that network equipment along the path prevented the media path from being established due to deep packet inspection rules.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-903">这可能是因为没有正确配置防火墙规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-903">This is likely due to firewall rules not being correctly configured.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-904">在此方案中，TCP 握手成功，但 SSL 握手未成功。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-904">In this scenario, the TCP handshake succeeded but the SSL handshake didn't.</span></span>      |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-905">缺少 FW IP 阻止例外规则</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-905">Missing FW IP Block Exception Rule</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-906">指示路径上的网络设备阻止将媒体路径建立到 Office 365 网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-906">Indicates that network equipment along the path prevented the media path from being established to the Office 365 network.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-907">这可能是因为未正确配置代理或防火墙规则，以便允许访问用于团队和 Skype for business 流量的 IP 地址和端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-907">This might be due to proxy or firewall rules not being correctly configured to allow access to IP addresses and ports used for Teams and Skype for Business traffic.</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-908">开始补救后，您可以将精力集中在特定建筑物或子网上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-908">Now as you begin your remediation, you can focus your efforts on a particular building or subnet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-909">如上表所示，这些问题是由于防火墙或代理配置导致的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-909">As the preceding table shows, these issues are due to firewall or proxy configurations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-910">查看下表中的选项以获取更正操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-910">Review the options in the following table for remediation actions.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-911">_表 8-通话设置失败修正的后续步骤_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-911">_Table 8 - Next Steps for Call Setup Failure Remediation_</span></span>


|      <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-912">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-912">Remediation</span></span>      |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-913">指引</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-913">Guidance</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
|-----------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-914">配置防火墙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-914">Configure firewall(s)</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-915">与您的网络团队协作，并针对[Office 365 IP 地址列表](https://aka.ms/o365ips)验证您的防火墙配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-915">Work with your network team and verify your firewall(s) configuration against [the Office 365 IP address list](https://aka.ms/o365ips).</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-916">验证防火墙规则中是否包含[媒体子网](https://support.office.com/article/Office-365-URLs-and-IP-address-ranges-8548a211-3fe7-47cb-abb1-355ea5aa88a2#bkmk_teams)和端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-916">Verify that the [media subnets](https://support.office.com/article/Office-365-URLs-and-IP-address-ranges-8548a211-3fe7-47cb-abb1-355ea5aa88a2#bkmk_teams) and ports are included in the firewall rules.</span></span> <br><br><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-917">验证是否在防火墙中打开了必要的端口（如下所示）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-917">Verify that the necessary ports (listed below) are opened in the firewall.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-918">UDP 应具有优先权，因为 TCP 被视为音频、视频和基于视频的屏幕共享的故障回复协议，其使用将影响呼叫的质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-918">UDP should be given priority because TCP is considered a failback protocol for audio, video, and video-based screen sharing, and its use will affect the quality of the call.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-919">旧版 RDP 应用程序共享仅使用 TCP。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-919">Legacy RDP application sharing uses TCP only.</span></span><br><ul><li><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-920">**TCP：** 端口443</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-920">**TCP:** port 443</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-921">**UDP：** 端口 3478-3481</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-921">**UDP:** ports 3478–3481</span></span></li><ul> |
|        <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-922">验证</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-922">Verify</span></span>         |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-923">使用 " [Microsoft 网络评估" 工具](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=53885)验证受影响的建筑物或子网的连接，方法是使用连接检查功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-923">Use the [Microsoft Network Assessment Tool](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=53885) to verify connectivity from the affected building or subnet by using the connectivity check function.</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |

### <a name="drop-failures"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-924">删除失败</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-924">Drop failures</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-925">与设置失败代码不同，CDQ 没有放置故障代码来指示为何出现放置失败，这使隔离特定的根本原因变得困难。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-925">Unlike setup failure codes, CDQ has no drop failure code to indicate why drop failures occur, which makes it difficult to isolate a specific root cause.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-926">若要更好地会审删除失败，请使用推断方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-926">To better triage drop failures, use an inferred approach.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-927">通过修正媒体的任何感兴趣的区域、修补客户端和驱动程序，并推动团队和 Skype for business 的认证设备的使用，您可能需要拒绝丢单。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-927">By remediating any areas of interest for media, patching clients and drivers, and driving usage of certified devices for Teams and Skype for Business, you can expect drop failures to decline.</span></span>

#### <a name="drop-failure-trend-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-928">丢放故障趋势分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-928">Drop failure trend analysis</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-929">此报告显示音频流、总丢单故障和下拉失败率的总数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-929">This report displays the total amount of audio streams, total drop failures, and the drop failure rate.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-930">指向任意一列以显示其值，如下图所示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-930">Point to any one of the columns to display its values, as shown in the following figure.</span></span> 

![显示已丢弃的流的百分比的图表](media/qerguide-image-droppedstreamrate.png)

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-932">_图 21-丢弃的流速率_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-932">_Figure 21 - Dropped stream rate_</span></span>

##### <a name="analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-933">定量分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-933">Analysis</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-934">通过使用此类报表，您可以回答以下问题：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-934">By using this type of report, you can answer the following questions:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-935">目前的击落故障率是多少？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-935">What is the current drop failure rate?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-936">丢单故障率是否低于定义的目标度量值？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-936">Is the drop failure rate below the defined target metric?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-937">故障趋势是否比上个月更糟或更好？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-937">Is the failure trend worse or better than the previous month?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-938">故障趋势是增长、稳定还是降低？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-938">Is the failure trend increasing, steady, or decreasing?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-939">无论上述问题的答案如何，都要花些时间研究一下使用子报表查找任何可能需要补救的建筑物或网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-939">Irrespective of the answers to the questions above, take the time to investigate using the sub-reports to look for any buildings or networks that might need remediation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-940">尽管整体放置故障率可能低于目标度量值，但一个或多个建筑物或网络的击落失败率可能高于目标指标，需要调查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-940">Although the overall drop failure rate might be below the target metric, the drop failure rate for one or more buildings or networks might be above the target metric and need investigation.</span></span>

#### <a name="drop-failure-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-941">删除失败调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-941">Drop failure investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-942">此处报告的故障表示呼叫被意外丢弃，并产生消极的用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-942">Failures reported here indicate that the call was dropped unexpectedly and resulted in a negative user experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-943">与趋势报告不同，这些报告提供了对需要进一步调查的特定子网的进一步见解。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-943">Unlike the trending reports, these reports provide additional insights into specific subnets that need further investigation.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-944">请确保将 "月份年份" 筛选器调整为当前月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-944">Be sure to adjust the Month Year filter to the current month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-945">选择 "**编辑**"，然后调整**月份年份**以保存新的默认月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-945">Select **Edit**, and adjust **Month Year** to save the new default month.</span></span>


![列出放置失败的次数和百分比的报表](media/qerguide-image-dropfailuresbysubnet.png)

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-947">_图22–通过子网丢弃故障_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-947">_Figure 22 – Drop failures by subnet_</span></span>

##### <a name="remediation"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-948">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-948">Remediation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-949">使用包含的表格报告，可以隔离网络中放置费率超过您定义的目标指标的问题区域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-949">Using the included table reports, you can isolate problem areas in the network where the drop rate is above the target metric you've defined.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-950">将您的第一项补救措施集中在具有最高总流计数的建筑物或子网上，以获得最大的影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-950">Focus your first remediation efforts on buildings or subnets that have the highest total stream count, to make the biggest impact.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-951">通话删除的常见原因：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-951">Common causes of call drops:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-952">预配网络或 internet 出口</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-952">Under-provisioned network or internet egress</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-953">未在受限制的网络上配置 QoS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-953">No QoS configured on constrained networks</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-954">较旧的客户端版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-954">Older client versions</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-955">用户行为</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-955">User behavior</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-956">发现你的问题区域后，你可以使用[调用分析](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309)进一步查看该构建中特定问题的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-956">After you discover your problem areas, you can use [Call Analytics](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309) to further review users in that building for specific issues.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-957">调用分析包含其他 PII 数据，并且对于进一步隔离放置失败的潜在原因非常有用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-957">Call Analytics contains additional PII data and can be useful for further isolating potential reasons for the drop failures.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-958">无论您的下一步如何，都是将已发现特定建筑物或子网的问题通知帮助台的好做法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-958">Regardless of your next step, it's a good practice to notify the helpdesk that an issue has been discovered with specific buildings or subnets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-959">通过这种方式，他们可以快速响应传入的呼叫并更高效地会审用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-959">This way, they can quickly respond to incoming calls and triage users more efficiently.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-960">然后，可向工程团队报告已标记的用户，以便进一步调查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-960">Flagged users can then be reported back to the engineering team for further investigation.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-961">下表列出了管理和修正丢弃故障的一些常用方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-961">The following table lists some common methods to manage and remediate drop failures.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-962">_表 9-通话丢弃补救措施的后续步骤_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-962">_Table 9 - Next steps for call drop remediation_</span></span>
