|------------------------------------------|-------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-965">**网络/互联网**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-965">**Network/internet**</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-966">**拥塞**：与你的网络团队协作以监控特定建筑物/子网的带宽，以确认是否存在使用过度的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-966">**Congestion**: Work with your network team to monitor bandwidth at specific buildings/subnets to confirm that there are issues with overutilization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-967">如果你确认存在网络拥塞，请考虑增加生成或应用 QoS 的带宽。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-967">If you do confirm that there is network congestion, consider increasing bandwidth to that building or applying QoS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-968">使用 "包含[质量较差的流摘要" 报表](#quality-investigations)查看问题子网中是否存在抖动、延迟和数据包丢失问题，因为它们通常位于放置的流之前。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-968">Use the included [Quality Poor Stream summary reports](#quality-investigations) to review the problem subnets for issues with jitter, latency, and packet loss, because these will often precede a dropped stream.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-969">**QoS**：如果增加的带宽不切实际或成本不受制约，请考虑实施 QoS。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-969">**QoS**: If increasing bandwidth is impractical or cost-prohibitive, consider implementing QoS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-970">此工具在管理拥塞的流量时非常有效，可确保托管网络上的媒体数据包优先于非媒体流量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-970">This tool is very effective at managing congested traffic and can guarantee that media packets on the managed network are prioritized above non-media traffic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-971">或者，如果没有明确的证据表明带宽是有原因的，请考虑以下解决方案：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-971">Alternatively, if there's no clear evidence that bandwidth is the culprit, consider these solutions:</span></span><ul><li>[<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-972">Microsoft 团队 QoS 指南</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-972">Microsoft Teams QoS guidance</span></span>](qos-in-teams.md)</li></ul><br><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-973">**执行网络准备情况评估**：网络评估提供有关预期带宽使用情况的详细信息，以及如何处理带宽和网络更改，以及团队和 Skype for business 的推荐联网做法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-973">**Perform a network readiness assessment**: A network assessment provides details about expected bandwidth usage, how to cope with bandwidth and network changes, and recommended networking practices for Teams and Skype for Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-974">将上一个表用作源，您有一个建筑物或子网的列表，它非常适合于评估。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-974">Using the preceding table as your source, you have a list of buildings or subnets that are excellent candidates for an assessment.</span></span><ul><li>[<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-975">Microsoft 团队网络准备情况评估</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-975">Microsoft Teams Network Readiness Assessment</span></span>](3-envision-evaluate-my-environment.md#test-the-network)</li></ul><br><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-976">**Microsoft 网络评估工具：** 使用此工具可对网络性能进行简单的测试，以确定网络对于团队或 Skype for business Online 呼叫的性能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-976">**Microsoft Network Assessment Tool:** Use this tool for a simple test of network performance to determine how well the network would perform for a Teams or Skype for Business Online call.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-977">该工具可帮助你评估子网的性能，并根据 Microsoft 性能[要求](https://aka.ms/performancerequirements)验证网络的准备情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-977">The tool helps you assess the performance of a subnet and validate the readiness of the network against Microsoft performance [requirements](https://aka.ms/performancerequirements).</span></span><ul><li>[<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-978">下载网络评估工具</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-978">Download the Network Assessment Tool</span></span>](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=53885)</li></ul> |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-979">**客户端（仅限 Skype for Business Online）**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-979">**Clients (Skype for Business Online only)**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-980">某些较旧的客户端存在媒体可靠性的已知、已记录的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-980">Some older clients have known, documented issues with media reliability.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-981">查看来自多个受影响用户的呼叫分析报告，或在 CQD 中创建自定义客户端版本表报表，筛选到具有总呼叫中断故障百分比的特定建筑物或子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-981">Review the Call Analytics reports from multiple affected users, or create a custom Client Version table report in CQD filtered to specific buildings or subnets with Total Call Dropped Failure % measure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-982">此信息将帮助你了解该特定建筑物和特定版本的客户端之间的通话中断之间是否存在关系。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-982">This information will help you understand whether a relationship exists between call drops in that specific building and a specific version of the client.</span></span>     |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-983">**Devices**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-983">**Devices**</span></span>                                  | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-984">我们建议，任何有呼叫中断的用户（一般情况下，使用集成设备）都应预配[经认证的耳机或免提电话](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs)，以将其排除在质量和可靠性较差的潜在来源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-984">We recommend that any users who are experiencing call drops—or poor calls in general—and are using integrated devices should be provisioned a [certified headset or speakerphone](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs)  to eliminate this as a potential source of poor quality and reliability.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-985">**用户行为**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-985">**User behavior**</span></span>                            | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-986">如果你确定不是网络、设备或客户端出现问题，请考虑制定用户采用策略来教育用户如何最大程度地加入和退出会议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-986">If you determine that neither network, devices, or clients are the issue, consider developing a user adoption strategy to educate users how to best join and exit meetings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-987">更智能的团队和 Skype for business 用户将为会议中的所有参与者提供更好的用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-987">A smarter Teams and Skype for Business user will produce a better user experience for all participants in the meeting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-988">将笔记本电脑置于睡眠状态（通过关闭盖子）而不退出会议的用户将被归类为意外的呼叫丢弃。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-988">A user who puts their laptop to sleep (by closing the lid) without exiting the meeting will be classified as an unexpected call drop.</span></span>   |

## <a name="quality-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-989">质量调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-989">Quality investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-990">在整个组织中评估音频质量状态的下一步是调查不良流速率（PSR.EXE）、TCP 和代理使用情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-990">The next step to assess the state of audio quality across the organization is to investigate Poor Stream Rate (PSR), TCP, and proxy usage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-991">请务必记住，CQD 数据不会为你提供特定的根本原因，而是向你提供可能的问题区域，以便开始与适用于补救活动的相应团队进行协作对话。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-991">It's important to remember that CQD data doesn't provide you a specific root cause, but instead provides you with likely problem areas to begin a collaborative conversation with the appropriate teams for remediation activities.</span></span> 

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-992">本指南不介绍这些模板中包含的所有报表;但是，下面介绍的调查方法仍适用于这些报表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-992">Not all reports included in the templates are covered in this guide; however, the methods of investigation explained below will still apply for those reports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-993">有关详细信息，请参阅各个报告说明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-993">Refer to the individual report description for more information.</span></span> 

### <a name="quality"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-994">画质</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-994">Quality</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-995">PSR.EXE 百分比用于指示组织是否为给定焦点区域的会议定义指标目标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-995">The PSR percentages are used to indicate whether the organization is meeting defined metric targets for a given focus area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-996">请务必注意，即使高级别的百分比位于定义的目标中，单个子网或建筑物可能不满足定义的目标，因此需要进一步调查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-996">It's important to note that even if the high-level percentages are within the defined target, individual subnets or buildings might not meet the defined targets and, therefore, need further investigation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-997">例如，如果整个音频 PSR.EXE 百分比是四月的2% （满足示例目标），则单个建筑物和子网可能仍然具有很差的体验，具体取决于该2百分比的整体分布。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-997">For example, if the overall audio PSR percentage is 2 percent in April, which meets the sample target, individual buildings and subnets might still be having poor experiences, depending on the overall distribution of that 2 percent.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-998">若要评估不良流的百分比，请使用质量报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-998">To assess the percentage of poor streams, use the quality reports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-999">提供了各种质量报告来查看整体、会议、两方、PSTN 呼叫、VPN 和会议室的指标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-999">Various quality reports are provided to review metrics for overall, conferencing, two-party, PSTN calling, VPN, and meeting rooms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1000">提供每月、每周和每日报表以帮助完成此过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1000">Monthly, weekly, and daily reports are provided to assist in this process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1001">每周和每日报表仅限于托管网络模板以提高其有效性并减少噪音。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1001">Weekly and daily reports are limited to the Managed Networks template to increase their effectiveness and reduce noise.</span></span> 

#### <a name="quality-trend-analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1002">质量趋势分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1002">Quality trend analysis</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1003">趋势报表显示一段时间内的质量信息，用于帮助识别和了解每个感兴趣领域的质量趋势。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1003">Trending reports display quality information over time and are used to help identify and understand quality trends within each area of interest.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1004">如上所述，模板中包含用于调查质量的报表树;会议、两方、PSTN 呼叫、VPN 和会议室。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1004">As noted above, there are report trees included in the templates for investigating quality; conferencing, two-party, PSTN calling, VPN, and meeting rooms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1005">出于分析质量的目的，调查过程是相同的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1005">For the purposes of analyzing quality, the investigative process is the same.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1006">但是，我们建议你首先从会议开始，因为对会议质量的任何改进也会对所有其他方面产生积极影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1006">However, we recommend that you start with conferencing first, because any improvements in conference quality will also positively affect all other areas.</span></span> 

> [!Note]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1007">调查两方、PSTN 呼叫和会议室与调查会议类似。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1007">Investigating two-party, PSTN calling, and meeting rooms are similar to investigating conferencing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1008">重点是 isloate 的建筑物或子网，其质量最差，并确定质量较差的原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1008">The focus is to isloate buildings or subnets that have the worst quality and identify the reason for the poor quality.</span></span>

> [!Important]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1009">基于 VPN 的报表使用第二个 VPN 维度进行筛选。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1009">VPN-based reports are filtered by using the Second VPN dimension.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1010">此维度要求 VPN 网络适配器正确注册为远程访问适配器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1010">This dimension requires that the VPN network adapter be properly registered as a Remote Access Adapter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1011">VPN 供应商不可靠地使用此标志，你的里程将根据你的组织中部署的 VPN 供应商而有所不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1011">VPN vendors don't reliably use this flag, and your mileage will vary depending on the VPN vendor deployed at your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1012">如果需要，请按照[本指南前面](#vpn)概述的指南使用建筑物或网络名称修改 VPN 报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1012">Follow the guidance outlined [earlier in this guide](#vpn) for modifying the VPN reports if needed by using the building or network name.</span></span>

![显示质量较差的流的百分比的图表](media/qerguide-image-audioqualityconferencing.png)

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1014">_图 23-音频质量-会议_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1014">_Figure 23 – Audio Quality - Conferencing_</span></span>

##### <a name="investigation"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1015">调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1015">Investigation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1016">通过使用这些报表，您可以回答以下问题：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1016">By using these reports, you can answer the following questions:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1017">当前月份的总 PSR.EXE 是多少？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1017">What is the total PSR for the current month?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1018">PSR.EXE 是否低于定义的目标度量？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1018">Is the PSR below the defined target metric?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1019">PSR.EXE 比上个月更糟还是更好？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1019">Is PSR worse or better than the previous month?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1020">PSR.EXE 趋势是增加、稳定还是减少？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1020">Is the PSR trend increasing, steady, or decreasing?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1021">无论上述问题的答案如何，都可以通过使用子报表查找任何可能需要调查的建筑物或子网来进行调查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1021">Irrespective of the answers to the questions above, take the time to investigate by using the sub-reports to look for any buildings or subnets that might need investigation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1022">尽管整体 PSR.EXE 可能位于目标度量的下方，但一个或多个建筑物或网络的 PSR.EXE 通常位于指标中，并且需要补救措施。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1022">Although the overall PSR might be below the target metric, often the PSR for one or more buildings or networks is above the metric and needs remediation.</span></span>

#### <a name="quality-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1023">质量调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1023">Quality investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1024">质量摘要报告让你更深入地了解将其分类为差的流，并有助于隔离托管网络中的问题区域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1024">The quality summary reports give you deeper insight into what contributed to the streams' being classified as poor and helps to isolate problem areas in the managed network.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1025">虽然使用的维度可能在报表之间稍有不同，但每个报表将包括用于流总数的度量值、总不良流、PSR.EXE 和因的质量较差。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1025">Although the dimensions used might differ slightly between report, each report will include measures for total streams, total poor streams, PSR, and poor quality due to.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1026">已为每个感兴趣的领域创建报表：会议、双方、PSTN 呼叫、VPN 和会议室。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1026">Reports have been created for each area of interest: conferencing, two-party, PSTN calling, VPN, and meeting rooms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1027">托管网络模板包含可利用通过生成文件上载的位置信息的其他报表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1027">The Managed Network template includes additional reports to take advantage of the location information uploaded via the building file.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1028">请确保将 "月份年份" 筛选器调整为当前月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1028">Be sure to adjust the Month Year filter to the current month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1029">选择 "**编辑**"，然后调整**月份年份**以保存新的默认月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1029">Select **Edit**, and adjust **Month Year** to save the new default month.</span></span>

> [!Note]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1030">由于公共子网的广泛使用，因此很难进行会审。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1030">Common subnets are difficult to triage due to their widespread use.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1031">显示客户的公共 IP （第二个自身本地 IP）的单独报告已添加到 "所有网络" 模板，以帮助使用常见网络的补救机构。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1031">A separate report that displays the client's public IP (Second Reflexive Local IP) has been added to the All Networks template to assist with remediating offices that use common networks.</span></span>


![显示较差音频流摘要的屏幕截图](media/qerguide-image-poorqualitysummary.png)

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1033">_图 24-通过构建和子网会议进行不良音频流摘要_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1033">_Figure 24 – Poor Audio Stream Summary by Building and Subnet - Conferencing_</span></span>

##### <a name="remediation"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1034">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1034">Remediation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1035">将您的补救措施集中在具有最大流量的建筑物或子网上，因为这样可以最大程度地提高影响，并有助于快速改进用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1035">Focus your remediation efforts on buildings or subnets that have the largest volume of streams, because this will maximize impact and help to improve the user experience quickly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1036">使用 "抖动"、"数据包丢失" 和 "往返时间（RTT）" 度量来了解对质量不佳的影响（可能存在多个问题）：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1036">Use the jitter, packet loss, and round-trip time (RTT) measurements to understand what's contributing to the poor quality (it's possible for there to be more than one problem):</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1037">**抖动**：媒体数据包以不同的速度到达，从而导致扬声器发声机器人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1037">**Jitter**: Media packets are arriving at different speeds, which causes a speaker to sound robotic.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1038">**数据包丢失**：丢弃媒体数据包，这会产生缺少单词或音节的效果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1038">**Packet loss**: Media packets are being dropped, which creates the effect of missing words or syllables.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1039">**RTT**：媒体数据包需要很长时间才能访问其目标，从而创建 walkie talkie 效果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1039">**RTT**: Media packets are taking a long time to get to their destination, which creates a walkie-talkie effect.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1040">为帮助您调查质量问题，您可以利用[呼叫分析](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1040">To assist your investigation into quality issues, you can leverage [Call Analytics](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1041">使用呼叫分析，您可以查看特定的会议或用户的详细呼叫报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1041">With Call Analytics, you can look at a specific conference or users' detailed call report.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1042">此报表将包含 PII 数据，在查找失败原因时很有用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1042">This report will contain PII data and is useful when you're looking for the cause of a failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1043">知道哪个生成受到影响后，在该建筑物中跟踪用户应该十分简单。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1043">After you know which building is affected, it should be straightforward to track down users in that building.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1044">不要忘记让帮助台知道这些网络遇到质量问题，因此他们可以快速对传入呼叫进行分类和响应。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1044">Don't forget to let the helpdesk know that these networks are experiencing quality issues, so they can quickly triage and respond to incoming calls.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1045">_表 10-高 PSR.EXE 的常见参与者_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1045">_Table 10 - Common contributors to high PSR_</span></span>

|------------------------------------------|----------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1048">**网络**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1048">**Networks**</span></span>                                 | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1049">**拥塞**：过度使用或未预配的网络可能会导致媒体质量问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1049">**Congestion**: An overused or under-provisioned network can cause issues with media quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1050">与网络团队协作，确定从用户到 internet 传出点的网络连接是否有足够的带宽来支持媒体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1050">Work with the network team to determine whether the network connections from the user to the internet egress point has enough bandwidth to support media.</span></span> <br><br><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1051">**执行网络准备情况评估**：网络评估提供有关预期带宽使用情况的详细信息，以及如何处理带宽和网络更改，以及团队和 Skype for business 的推荐联网做法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1051">**Perform a network readiness assessment**: A network assessment provides details about expected bandwidth usage, how to cope with bandwidth and network changes, and recommended networking practices for Teams and Skype for Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1052">将上一个表用作源，您有一个建筑物或子网的列表，它非常适合于评估。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1052">Using the preceding table as your source, you have a list of buildings or subnets that are excellent candidates for an assessment.</span></span><ul><li>[<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1053">Microsoft 团队网络准备情况评估</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1053">Microsoft Teams Network Readiness Assessment</span></span>](3-envision-evaluate-my-environment.md#test-the-network)</li></ul><br><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1054">**Microsoft 网络评估工具：** 使用此工具可对网络性能进行简单的测试，以确定网络对于团队或 Skype for business Online 呼叫的性能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1054">**Microsoft Network Assessment Tool:** Use this tool for a simple test of network performance to determine how well the network would perform for a Teams or Skype for Business Online call.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1055">该工具可帮助你评估子网的性能，并根据 Microsoft 性能[要求](https://aka.ms/performancerequirements)验证网络的准备情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1055">The tool helps you assess the performance of a subnet and validate the readiness of the network against Microsoft performance [requirements](https://aka.ms/performancerequirements).</span></span><ul><li>[<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1056">下载网络评估工具</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1056">Download the Network Assessment Tool</span></span>](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=53885)</li></ul><br> |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1057">**服务质量 (QoS)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1057">**Quality of Service (QoS)**</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1058">QoS 是一种经验证的工具，可帮助在拥挤的网络上优先处理数据包，确保它们的目标时间和时间保持不变。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1058">QoS is a proven tool to help prioritize packets on a congested network to ensure they arrive at their destination intact and on time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1059">考虑在整个组织中实施 QoS，最大程度地提高用户在带宽受到限制的体验的质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1059">Consider implementing QoS across your organization to maximize the quality of the user experience where bandwidth is constrained.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1060">QoS 将帮助解决与数据包丢失较高的问题（通常与较低程度）相关的问题：抖动和往返行程时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1060">QoS will help solve issues typically associated with high levels of packet loss, and—to a lesser degree—jitter and round-trip times.</span></span><ul><li>[<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1061">Microsoft 团队 QoS 指南</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1061">Microsoft Teams QoS guidance</span></span>](qos-in-teams.md)</li></ul> |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1062">**Wi-Fi**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1062">**Wi-Fi**</span></span>               | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1063">Wi-fi 可能会对通话质量产生重大影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1063">Wi-Fi can have a significant impact on call quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1064">Wi-fi 部署通常不考虑 VoIP 服务的网络要求，并且通常是质量较差的来源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1064">Wi-Fi deployments don't typically take into consideration the network requirements for VoIP services and are often a source of poor quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1065">有关优化 Wlan 基础结构的详细信息，请参阅[有关 wi-fi 计划的文章](/skypeforbusiness/certification/plan-wifi)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1065">For more information about optimizing your Wi-Fi infrastructure, see [this article about Wi-Fi planning](/skypeforbusiness/certification/plan-wifi).</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1066">**无线驱动程序**：确保无线驱动程序是最新的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1066">**Wireless driver**: Ensure that wireless drivers are up to date.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1067">这将有助于减少与过时驱动程序相关的任何不良用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1067">This will help mitigate any poor user experience related to an outdated driver.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1068">许多组织不在其修补程序周期内包含无线驱动程序，这些驱动程序可能会在几年后再进行修补。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1068">Many organizations don't include wireless drivers in their patch cycles, and these drivers can go unpatched for years.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1069">通过确保无线驱动程序处于最新状态，解决了许多无线问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1069">Many wireless issues are solved by ensuring the wireless drivers are up to date.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1070">**WMM**：无线多媒体扩展（WMM）（也称为 wi-fi 多媒体）为无线网络提供基本 QoS 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1070">**WMM**: Wireless Multimedia Extensions (WMM), also known as Wi-Fi Multimedia, provides basic QoS features to wireless networks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1071">新式无线网络必须支持许多设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1071">Modern wireless networks must support many devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1072">这些设备争用带宽，并且可能会导致 VoIP 服务的质量问题，其中的速度和延迟非常重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1072">These devices compete for bandwidth and can lead to quality issues for VoIP services, where speed and latency are vital.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1073">有关详细信息，请咨询您的无线供应商，并考虑在无线网络上实施 WMM，以确定 Skype for business 和团队媒体的优先级。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1073">Consult your wireless vendor for specifics and consider implementing WMM on your wireless network to prioritize Skype for Business and Teams media.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1074">**接入点密度**：接入点可能会在理想位置中相隔太远或不在理想位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1074">**Access point density**: Access points might be too far apart or not in an ideal location.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1075">若要最大程度地减少潜在干扰，请在会议室中以及不受墙壁或其他物体阻碍的位置（即 Wi-fi 信号较弱的位置）放置额外的访问点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1075">To minimize potential interference, place extra access points in conference rooms and in locations that aren't obstructed by walls or other objects where the Wi-Fi signal is weak.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1076">**2.4 ghz 与 5 ghz**： 5 ghz 提供较少的后台干扰和更高的速度，并且应在通过 Wi-fi 部署 VoIP 时进行优先级划分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1076">**2.4 GHz versus 5 GHz**: 5 GHz provides less background interference and higher speeds, and should be prioritized when deploying VoIP over Wi-Fi.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1077">但是，5 GHz 不像 2.4 GHz 那样强大，并且不会很轻松地穿透墙壁。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1077">However, 5 GHz isn't as strong as 2.4 GHz and doesn't penetrate walls as easily.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1078">查看建筑物布局以确定你可以为最佳连接所依赖的频率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1078">Review your building layout to determine which frequency you can rely on for the best connection.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1079">**网络设备**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1079">**Network device**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1080">较大的组织可能会在网络上分布数百个设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1080">Larger organizations might have hundreds of devices spread out across the network.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1081">与您的网络团队协作，确保从用户到 internet 的网络设备保持最新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1081">Work with your network team to ensure that the network devices from the user to the internet are maintained and up to date.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1082">**VPN**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1082">**VPN**</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1083">VPN 装置传统上不会用于处理实时媒体工作负荷。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1083">VPN appliances aren't traditionally designed to handle real-time media workloads.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1084">某些 VPN 配置禁止使用 UDP （这是媒体的首选协议），并且仅依赖于 TCP。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1084">Some VPN configurations prohibit the use of UDP (which is the preferred protocol for media) and rely on TCP only.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1085">请考虑实现 VPN 拆分隧道解决方案，以帮助将 VPN 减少为质量较差的源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1085">Consider implementing a VPN split-tunnel solution to help reduce VPN as a source of poor quality.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1086">**客户端**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1086">**Clients**</span></span> <br><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1087">（仅限 Skype for Business Online）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1087">(Skype for Business Online only)</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1088">确保定期更新所有客户端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1088">Ensure all clients are being regularly updated.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1089">**Devices**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1089">**Devices**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1090">使用优化的[设备](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog)可帮助显著改善用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1090">The use of [optimized devices](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog) can help to significantly improve the user experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1091">随着所有方面的要求，优化的设备旨在最大限度地提高团队和 Skype for business 的用户体验，并产生优质的质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1091">With all things being equal, optimized devices are designed to maximize the user experience with Teams and Skype for Business, and produce superior quality.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1092">**设备**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1092">**Drivers**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1093">修补网络（以太网和 Wi-fi）、音频、视频和 USB 驱动程序应该是整个修补程序管理策略的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1093">Patching network (Ethernet and Wi-Fi), audio, video, and USB drivers should be part of your overall patch management strategy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1094">通过更新驱动程序解决了许多质量问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1094">Many quality issues are solved by updating drivers.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1095">**Wi-fi 上的会议室**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1095">**Meeting rooms on Wi-Fi**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1096">我们强烈建议使用至少 1 Gbps 以太网连接将会议室设备连接到网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1096">We highly recommend that meeting room devices be connected to the network by using at least a 1-Gbps Ethernet connection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1097">会议室设备通常包括多个音频和视频流以及会议内容（如屏幕共享），并且比其他团队或 Skype for business 终结点具有更高的网络要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1097">Meeting room devices typically include multiple audio and video streams, along with meeting content such as screen sharing, and have higher network requirements than other Teams or Skype for Business endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1098">根据定义，会议室在安装期间仅提供一个福利的固定设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1098">Meeting rooms are, by definition, stationary devices where Wi-Fi affords a benefit only during installation.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1099">会议室需要进行额外的关注，以确保使用这些设备的体验达到或超过预期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1099">Meeting rooms need to be treated with extra care and attention to ensure that the experience using these devices is meeting or exceeding expectations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1100">会议室的质量问题通常会快速升级，因为它们通常由高级人员使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1100">Quality issues with meeting rooms are usually going to be escalated quickly, because they're often used by senior-level staff.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1101">所有内容相等（除了方便），Wi-fi 性能通常小于有线连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1101">With all things being equal (apart from convenience), Wi-Fi performance is often less than a wired connection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1102">随着 "携带您自己的设备" 政策和笔记本电脑的普及，Wi-fi 接入点通常会过度使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1102">With the rise of "bring your own device" policies and the proliferation of laptops, Wi-Fi access points are often over-utilized.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1103">实时媒体可能不会在 Wi-fi 网络上优先，这可能会导致在高峰使用时间内出现质量问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1103">Real-time media might not be prioritized on Wi-Fi networks, which can lead to quality issues during peak use times.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1104">这种繁重的用法可能会与会议中可能有十二个人的会议相符，每个人都有自己的膝上型电脑和智能手机，并且均连接到与会议室设备相同的 Wi-fi 接入点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1104">This heavy usage can coincide with a meeting where there might be a dozen people in attendance, each with their own laptop and smartphone, all connected to the same Wi-Fi access point as the meeting room device.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1105">仅在手机安装时，也应将 wi-fi 视为临时解决方案，或者在已正确设置 Wi-fi 以支持企业级的实时媒体时。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1105">Wi-Fi should only be considered as a temporary solution, for a mobile installation, or when Wi-Fi has been properly provisioned to support business-class, real-time–based media.</span></span> |


### <a name="tcp"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1106">TCP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1106">TCP</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1107">TCP 被视为 "回切传输"，而不是你想要用于实时媒体的主传输。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1107">TCP is considered a failback transport and not the primary transport you want for real-time media.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1108">其故障回复传输的原因是 TCP 的状态特点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1108">The reason it's a failback transport is due to the stateful nature of TCP.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1109">例如，如果在潜在的网络上进行呼叫，并且媒体数据包被延迟，而不是在几秒钟前（这些数据包将不再有用），则会对带宽进行竞争以访问接收器，这可能会导致较差的情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1109">For example, if a call is made on a latent network and media packets are delayed, then packets from a few seconds ago—which are no longer useful—compete for bandwidth to get to the receiver, which can make a bad situation worse.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1110">这将使音频 healer 缝合和拉伸音频，从而产生可听见的项目，通常采用抖动形式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1110">This makes the audio healer stitch and stretch audio, resulting in audible artifacts, often in the form of jitter.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1111">本部分中的报表不区分良好流和不良流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1111">The reports in this section don't make a distinction between good and poor streams.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1112">鉴于使用 UDP，报表将查找对音频、视频和基于视频的屏幕共享（VBSS）的 TCP 的使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1112">Given that UDP is preferred, the reports look for the use of TCP for audio, video, and video-based screen sharing (VBSS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1113">提供的流费率较差有助于比较 UDP 质量与 TCP 质量，以便你可以专注于影响最大的工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1113">Poor stream rates are provided to help compare UDP quality versus TCP quality so that you can focus your efforts where the impact is the greatest.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1114">TCP 用法主要由不完整的防火墙规则所导致。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1114">TCP usage is primarily caused by incomplete firewall rules.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1115">有关团队和 Skype for Business Online 的防火墙规则的详细信息，请参阅[Office 365 url 和 IP 地址范围](https://aka.ms/o365ips)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1115">For more information about firewall rules for Teams and Skype for Business Online, see [Office 365 URLs and IP address ranges](https://aka.ms/o365ips).</span></span>

> [!Important]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1116">强烈建议上载一个[有效的生成文件](#building-mapping)，以便你可以在查看 TCP 使用时快速区分外部流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1116">Having a [valid building file](#building-mapping) uploaded is highly recommended so you can quickly distinguish inside from outside streams when looking at TCP usage.</span></span>

> [!Note]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1117">音频、视频和 VBSS 所有首选 UDP 作为其主传输。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1117">Audio, video, and VBSS all prefer UDP as their primary transport.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1118">旧版 RDP 应用程序共享工作负荷仅使用 TCP。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1118">The legacy RDP Application Sharing workload only uses TCP.</span></span>

#### <a name="tcp-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1119">TCP 使用情况</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1119">TCP usage</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1120">TCP 报表表示过去七个月内的总 TCP 使用率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1120">TCP reports indicates the overall TCP usage over the last seven months.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1121">本部分中的所有进一步报表将重点介绍最常使用 TCP 的特定建筑物和子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1121">All further reports in this section will focus on narrowing down specific buildings and subnets where TCP is most commonly used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1122">单独的报表可用于会议和两方流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1122">Separate reports are available for both conferencing and two-party streams.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1123">![图表显示使用 tcp](media/qerguide-image-audiostreamswithtcp.png)
图25的音频流百分比（使用_tcp 使用的音频流）_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1123">![Chart showing the percentage of audio streams that use TCP](media/qerguide-image-audiostreamswithtcp.png)

##### <a name="investigation"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1124">调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1124">Investigation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1125">通过使用此报表，你可以回答以下问题：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1125">By using this report, you can answer the following questions:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1126">当前月份的 TCP 流总容量是多少？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1126">What is the total volume of TCP streams for the current month?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1127">它是否比上个月更糟或更好？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1127">Is it worse or better than the previous month?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1128">TCP 使用趋势是增加、稳定还是减少？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1128">Is the TCP usage trend increasing, steady, or decreasing?</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1129">TCP PSR.EXE 是否与我的总 PSR.EXE？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1129">Is the TCP PSR the same as my overall PSR?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1130">如果你注意到，TCP 使用趋势增加或高于正常的每月使用时间，请通过使用子报表来查找可能需要补救的任何建筑物或网络，以进行调查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1130">If you notice that the TCP usage trend is increasing or above normal monthly usage, take the time to investigate by using the sub-reports to look for any buildings or networks that might need remediation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1131">理想情况下，你希望在托管网络上尽可能少的基于 TCP 的音频会话。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1131">Ideally, you want as few TCP-based audio sessions as possible on the managed network.</span></span>

#### <a name="tcp-vs-udp"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1132">TCP 与 UDP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1132">TCP vs. UDP</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1133">此报表标识基于音频、视频和基于视频的屏幕共享（VBSS）的最新月的 TCP 和 UDP 使用情况报告的数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1133">This report identifies the volume of TCP versus UDP usage reporting on the latest month for audio, video, and video-based screen sharing (VBSS).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1135">_图 26-TCP 与 UDP-会议_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1135">_Figure 26 – TCP vs. UDP - Conferencing_</span></span>

##### <a name="analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1136">定量分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1136">Analysis</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1137">尽管你希望 TCP 使用率尽可能低，但你可能会在其他正常的部署中看到一些 TCP 用法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1137">Although you want TCP usage to be as low as possible, you might see a bit of TCP usage in an otherwise healthy deployment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1138">TCP 本身不会影响较差的调用，因此提供了流速率以帮助确定 TCP 使用是否是影响质量较差的参与者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1138">TCP by itself won't contribute to a poor call, so stream rates are provided to help identify whether TCP usage is a contributor to poor quality.</span></span> 

#### <a name="tcp-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1139">TCP 调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1139">TCP investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1140">在提供的 CQD 模板中，通过使用 "托管网络" 或 "所有网络" 模板构建和子网报告，导航到 TCP 流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1140">In the provided CQD templates, navigate to the TCP Streams by Building and Subnet reports by using either the Managed Networks or All Networks template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1141">为了调查 TCP 使用，流程是相同的，因此我们将重点介绍有关会议的讨论。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1141">For the purpose of investigating TCP usage, the process is the same, so we'll focus the discussion here on conferencing.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1142">建议上载一个有效的[生成文件](#building-mapping)，以便你可以在查看 TCP 使用时快速从流外部进行区分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1142">Having a valid [building file](#building-mapping) uploaded is recommended so you can quickly distinguish inside from outside streams when looking at TCP usage.</span></span> 

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1143">请确保将 "月份年份" 筛选器调整为当前月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1143">Be sure to adjust the Month Year filter to the current month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1144">选择 "**编辑**"，然后调整**月份年份**以保存新的默认月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1144">Select **Edit**, and adjust **Month Year** to save the new default month.</span></span>                                  |

![通过构建和子网进行 TCP 使用的屏幕截图](media/qerguide-image-tcpstreams.png)

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1146">_图 27-通过构建和子网会议的 TCP 流_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1146">_Figure 27 – TCP Streams by Building and Subnet - Conferencing_</span></span>

##### <a name="remediation"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1147">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1147">Remediation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1148">此报表标识对 TCP 使用量有影响的特定建筑物和子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1148">This report identifies specific buildings and subnets that are contributing to the volume of TCP usage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1149">还包含一个其他报告，用于识别在通话中使用的 Microsoft 中继 IP，以帮助隔离缺少的防火墙规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1149">An additional report is also included to identify the Microsoft Relay IP that was used in the call to help isolate missing firewall rules.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1150">将您的补救措施集中在具有最高 TCP 流数量的建筑物上，以最大限度地提高影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1150">Focus your remediation efforts on those buildings that have the highest volume of TCP streams to maximize impact.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1151">TCP 使用的最常见原因是防火墙或代理中缺少例外规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1151">The most common cause of TCP usage is missing exception rules in firewalls or proxies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1152">我们将在下一节中讨论有关代理的信息，以便我们将精力集中在防火墙上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1152">We'll be talking about proxies in the next section, so for now focus your efforts on the firewalls.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1153">通过使用提供的建筑物或子网，你可以确定需要更新的防火墙。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1153">By using the building or subnet provided, you can determine which firewall needs to be updated.</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1154">_表 11-通过构建和子网进行 TCP 流的补救指南_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1154">_Table 11 - Remediation guidance for TCP streams by building and subnet_</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1155">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1155">Remediation</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1156">指引</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1156">Guidance</span></span>     |
|--------------------|--------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1157">配置防火墙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1157">Configure firewall</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1158">验证是否已从防火墙中排除[Office 365 IP 端口和地址](https://aka.ms/o365ips)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1158">Verify that [Office 365 IP ports and addresses](https://aka.ms/o365ips) are excluded from your firewall.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1159">对于与媒体相关的 TCP 问题，请重点关注以下各项的初始工作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1159">For media-related TCP issues, focus your initial efforts on the following:</span></span><ul><li><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1160">验证客户端媒体子网 13.107.64.0/18 和 52.112.0.0/14 是否在你的防火墙规则中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1160">Verify that the client media subnets 13.107.64.0/18 and 52.112.0.0/14 are in your firewall rules.</span></span></li><li><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1161">UDP 端口 3478-3481 是所需的媒体端口，必须打开，否则客户端将故障回复到 TCP 端口443。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1161">UDP ports 3478–3481 are the required media ports and must be opened, otherwise the client will fail back to TCP port 443.</span></span></li></ul> |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1162">验证</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1162">Verify</span></span>             | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1163">使用[Microsoft 网络评估工具](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=53885)检查与受影响的建筑物或子网中的特定 OFFICE 365 IP 地址和端口的连接问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1163">Use the [Microsoft Network Assessment Tool](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=53885) to check for issues with connectivity to specific Office 365 IP addresses and ports from the affected building or subnet.</span></span>    |

### <a name="http-proxy"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1164">HTTP 代理</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1164">HTTP proxy</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1165">出于多种原因，HTTP 代理不是用于建立媒体会话的首选路径。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1165">HTTP proxies aren't the preferred path for establishing media sessions, for a multitude of reasons.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1166">其中许多包含有助于防止服务连接完成并导致中断的深层数据包检查功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1166">Many contain deep packet inspection features that can prevent connections to the service from being completed and introduce disruptions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1167">此外，几乎所有的代理都强制使用 TCP，而不是允许使用 UDP，这是为了获得最佳音频质量而建议的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1167">Additionally, almost all proxies force TCP as opposed to allowing UDP, which is recommended for optimal audio quality.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1168">我们始终建议你将客户端配置为直接连接到团队和 Skype for Business 服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1168">We always recommend that you configure the client to directly connect to Teams and Skype for Business services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1169">这对于基于媒体的流量尤其重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1169">This is especially important for media-based traffic.</span></span>


> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1170">在上载了有效的[生成文件](#building-mapping)后，可以轻松地在分析代理使用情况时将外部音频流与外部音频流区分开来。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1170">Having a valid [building file](#building-mapping) uploaded makes it easy to properly distinguish inside from outside audio streams when analyzing proxy usage.</span></span> 


#### <a name="http-proxy-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1171">HTTP 代理使用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1171">HTTP proxy usage</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1172">模板的此部分中的 HTTP 代理流报告非常类似于 TCP 报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1172">The HTTP proxy stream report in this section of the template is much like the TCP reports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1173">它不会查看通话是否很差或是否良好，但呼叫是否通过 HTTP 连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1173">It doesn't look at whether calls are poor or good, but whether the call is connected over HTTP.</span></span>

![使用 HTTP 的音频流的报告的屏幕截图](media/qerguide-image-audiostreamswithhttp.png)

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1175">_图 28-具有 HTTP 代理使用的音频流_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1175">_Figure 28 – Audio Streams with HTTP Proxy Usage_</span></span>

##### <a name="analysis"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1176">定量分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1176">Analysis</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1177">你希望查看尽可能少的 HTTP 媒体流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1177">You want to see as little HTTP media streams as possible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1178">如果你有流遍历你的代理，请咨询你的网络团队以确保正确的排除，以便客户直接路由到团队或 Skype for business Online 媒体子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1178">If you have streams traversing your proxy, consult your networking team to ensure that the proper exclusions are in place so that clients are directly routing to Teams or Skype for Business Online media subnets.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1179">如果你的组织中只有一个 internet 代理，请验证正确的[Office 365 url 和 IP 地址范围排除](https://aka.ms/o365ips)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1179">If you have only one internet proxy in your organization, verify the proper [Office 365 URLs and IP address range exclusions](https://aka.ms/o365ips).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1180">如果您的组织中配置了多个 internet 代理，请使用 HTTP 子报告隔离受影响的建筑物或子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1180">If more than one internet proxy is configured in your organization, use the HTTP sub-report to isolate which building or subnet is affected.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1181">对于无法绕过代理的组织，请确保将 Skype for business 客户端配置为在代理之后正确登录，如下所述： [skype For business 应使用代理服务器登录，而不是尝试直接连接](https://support.microsoft.com/help/3207112/skype-for-business-should-use-proxy-server-to-sign-in-instead-of-tryin)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1181">For organizations that can't bypass the proxy, ensure that the Skype for Business client is configured to sign in properly when it's located behind a proxy, as outlined in the article [Skype for Business should use proxy server to sign in instead of trying direct connection](https://support.microsoft.com/help/3207112/skype-for-business-should-use-proxy-server-to-sign-in-instead-of-tryin).</span></span> 


#### <a name="http-proxy-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1182">HTTP 代理调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1182">HTTP proxy investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1183">此报告标识了对 HTTP 使用情况所造成的特定建筑物和子网。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1183">This report identifies specific buildings and subnets that are contributing to HTTP usage.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1184">在上载了有效的[生成文件](#building-mapping)后，可以轻松地在分析代理使用情况时将外部音频流与外部音频流区分开来。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1184">Having a valid [building file](#building-mapping) uploaded makes it easy to properly distinguish inside from outside audio streams when analyzing proxy usage.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1185">请确保将 "月份年份" 筛选器调整为当前月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1185">Be sure to adjust the Month Year filter to the current month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1186">选择 "**编辑**"，然后调整**月份年份**以保存新的默认月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1186">Select **Edit**, and adjust **Month Year** to save the new default month.</span></span>

##### <a name="remediation"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1189">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1189">Remediation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1190">我们[建议](proxy-servers-for-skype-for-business-online.md)您始终绕过 Skype for Business 和团队（尤其是媒体流量）的代理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1190">We [recommend](proxy-servers-for-skype-for-business-online.md) that you always bypass proxies for Skype for Business and Teams, especially media traffic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1191">代理不会使 Skype for business 更安全，因为其流量已加密。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1191">Proxies don't make Skype for Business more secure, because its traffic is already encrypted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1192">环境中可能会出现由于延迟和数据包丢失而引起的与性能相关的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1192">Performance-related problems can be introduced to the environment through latency and packet loss.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1193">此类问题将导致具有音频、视频和屏幕共享的消极体验，其中实时流非常重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1193">Issues such as these will result in a negative experience with audio, video and screen sharing, where real-time streams are essential.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1194">HTTP 使用的最常见原因是代理中缺少异常规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1194">The most common cause of HTTP usage is missing exception rules in proxies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1195">通过使用提供的建筑物或子网，你可以快速确定需要为媒体绕过配置的代理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1195">By using the building or subnet provided, you can quickly determine which proxy needs to be configured for media bypass.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1196">验证代理中是否列入白名单中所需的[Office 365 fqdn](https://aka.ms/o365ips) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1196">Verify that the required [Office 365 FQDNs](https://aka.ms/o365ips) are whitelisted in your proxy.</span></span>

## <a name="endpoint-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1197">终结点调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1197">Endpoint investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1198">本部分重点介绍用于报告客户端版本和使用已认证设备的任务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1198">This section is focused on the tasks for reporting on client versions and the use of certified devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1199">报告可用于客户端版本、客户端类型、捕获设备和驱动程序（麦克风）、视频捕获设备和 Wlan 供应商和驱动程序版本的大纲使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1199">Reports are available to outline usage for client versions, client type, capture devices and drivers (microphone), video capture devices, and Wi-Fi vendor and driver versions.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1200">本指南不介绍这些模板中包含的所有报表;但是，下面介绍的调查方法仍适用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1200">Not all reports included in the templates are covered in this guide; however, the methods of investigation explained below still apply.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1201">有关详细信息，请参阅各个报告说明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1201">Refer to the individual report description for more information.</span></span>

### <a name="client-versions"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1202">客户端版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1202">Client versions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1203">此空间中的报表重点介绍如何识别正在使用的 Skype for business 客户端版本以及它们在环境中的相对音量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1203">The reports in this space focus on identifying Skype for Business client versions in use and their relative volume in the environment.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1204">当前，团队客户通过 Azure 内容交付网络自动分发和更新，并将由服务保持最新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1204">Currently, Teams clients are distributed and updated automatically through the Azure Content Delivery Network and will be kept up to date by the service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1205">客户端准备情况和调查活动不适用于团队。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1205">Client readiness and investigative activities aren't applicable to Teams.</span></span>

> [!Important]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1206">除非你排除联盟参与者数据，否则这些报表将包含来自联合终结点的客户端遥测。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1206">Unless you exclude federated participant data, these reports will include client telemetry from federated endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1207">若要排除联合终结点，必须为设置为组织的[租户 id](#tenant-id)的第二租户 id 添加[查询筛选器](#query-filters)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1207">To exclude federated endpoints, you must add a [query filter](#query-filters) for Second Tenant ID set to your organization's [tenant ID](#tenant-id).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1208">或者，你可以使用[URL 筛选器](#url-filter)来排除联合参与者遥测。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1208">Alternatively, you can use a [URL filter](#url-filter) to exclude federated participant telemetry.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1209">请确保将 "月份年份" 筛选器调整为当前月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1209">Be sure to adjust the Month Year filter to the current month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1210">选择 "**编辑**"，然后调整**月份年份**以保存新的默认月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1210">Select **Edit**, and adjust **Month Year** to save the new default month.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1212">_图 30-客户端版本报告_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1212">_Figure 30 - Client version report_</span></span>

#### <a name="remediation"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1213">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1213">Remediation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1214">驱动高质量的用户体验的一个重要部分是确保托管客户在运行最新版本的 Skype for business 时，除了确保支持的音频、视频、网络和 USB 驱动程序都是最新版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1214">A critical part of driving high-quality user experiences is ensuring that managed clients are running up-to-date versions of Skype for Business, in addition to ensuring the supporting audio, video, network, and USB drivers are up to date.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1215">这提供了多项好处，其中包括：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1215">This provides several benefits, among them:</span></span> 

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1216">更易于管理几个版本，而不是许多版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1216">It's easier to manage a few versions versus many versions.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1217">它提供经验的一致性级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1217">It provides a level of consistency of experience.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1218">它使解决通话质量和可用性问题变得更容易。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1218">It makes it easier to troubleshoot problems with call quality and usability.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1219">Microsoft 不断对整个产品进行总体改进和优化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1219">Microsoft continually makes general improvements and optimizations across the product.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1220">确保用户收到这些更新会降低其遇到已解决问题的风险。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1220">Ensuring that users receive these updates reduces their risk of running into a problem that has already been solved.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1221">将部署限制为不超过六个月的客户端版本将通过减少需要支持的版本的数量来改善整体用户体验并提高可管理性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1221">Limiting your deployment to client versions that are less than six months old will improve the overall user experience and improve manageability by reducing the number of versions that need to be supported.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1222">如果您仅使用 Office 即点即用，您将在 "六个月" 窗口中自动显示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1222">If you're using only Office Click-to-Run, you'll automatically be within the six-month window.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1223">无需执行进一步操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1223">No further action is required.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1224">如果你有混合的即点即用和安装程序包（MSI），则可以使用该报告验证是否定期更新 MSI 客户端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1224">If you have a mix of Click-to-Run and installer packages (MSI), you can use the report to verify that the MSI clients are being updated regularly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1225">如果你发现客户端的进度落后，请与负责管理 Office 更新的团队协作，确保他们定期批准和部署客户端修补程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1225">If you notice clients are falling behind, work with the team responsible for managing Office updates and ensure that they're approving and deploying client patches regularly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1226">还必须考虑并确保网络、视频、USB 和音频驱动程序也能进行修补。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1226">It's also important to consider and ensure that the network, video, USB, and audio drivers are being patched as well.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1227">可轻松忽略这些驱动程序，不将它们包含在修补程序管理策略中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1227">It can be easy to overlook these drivers and not include them in your patch management strategy.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1228">Skype for Business 的版本号可通过以下链接找到：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1228">Version numbers for Skype for Business can be found via the links below:</span></span>

-   [<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1229">Office 专业增强版更新的发布信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1229">Release information for updates to Office ProPlus</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/officeupdates/release-notes-office365-proplus)
-   [<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1230">适用于企业的 Microsoft 365 应用的更新历史记录</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1230">Update history for Microsoft 365 Apps for enterprise</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/officeupdates/update-history-office365-proplus-by-date)
-   [<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1231">Skype for Business 下载和更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1231">Skype for Business downloads and updates</span></span>](/SkypeForBusiness/software-updates)

### <a name="devices"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1232">设备</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1232">Devices</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1233">若要使用麦克风设备报表，我们需要了解平均观点（MOS）的概念。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1233">To make use of the microphone device report, we need to understand the concept of the mean opinion score (MOS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1234">MOS 是用于测量所看到的音频质量的金牌标准测量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1234">MOS is the gold-standard measurement to gauge the perceived audio quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1235">它表示为从0到5的整数分级。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1235">It's represented as an integer rating from 0 to 5.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1236">语音质量的所有方法的基础是人员如何感觉语音质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1236">The basis of all measures of voice quality is how a person perceives the quality of speech.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1237">因为它受人类认知的影响，因此它本身是主观的主观。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1237">Because it's affected by human perception, it's inherently subjective.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1238">有多种不同的主观测试方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1238">There are several different methodologies for subjective testing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1239">大多数语音质量指标基于绝对分类分级（ACR）缩放。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1239">Most voice quality measures are based on an absolute categorization rating (ACR) scale.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1240">在 ACR 主观测试中，统计数量很多的人按1（坏）到5（很好）的费率对体验质量进行了评级。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1240">In an ACR subjective test, a statistically significant number of people rate their quality of experience on a scale of 1 (bad) to 5 (excellent).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1241">分数的平均值为 MOS。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1241">The average of the scores is the MOS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1242">所得到的 MOS 取决于向组公开的体验范围以及要评级的体验类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1242">The resulting MOS depends on the range of experiences that were exposed to the group and to the type of experience being rated.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1243">由于对实时通信系统执行语音质量的主观测试是不切实际的，Microsoft 团队和 Skype for business 通过使用高级算法客观预测主观测试的结果来生成 MOS 值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1243">Because it's impractical to conduct subjective tests of voice quality for a live communication system, Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business generate MOS values by using advanced algorithms to objectively predict the results of a subjective test.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1244">可用的 MOS 和相关指标集提供了一种视图，可查看由音频设备向用户发送的体验的质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1244">The available set of MOS and associated metrics provide a view into the quality of the experience being delivered to the users by an audio device.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1245">通过向用户提供针对团队和 Skype for business 认证的设备，你可以降低因设备本身而产生负面体验的可能性（例如，内置的便携式扬声器和麦克风更有可能）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1245">By supplying users with devices certified for Teams and Skype for Business, you reduce the likelihood of encountering negative experiences due to the device itself (which is more likely, for example, with built-in laptop speakers and microphones).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1246">有关详细信息，请参阅[认证计划](/SkypeForBusiness/certification/overview)和[合作伙伴解决方案目录](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs)中的这些文章。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1246">For more information, see these articles on the [certification program](/SkypeForBusiness/certification/overview) and the [partner solutions catalog](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1247">设备报表用于按音量和 MOS 评分（仅限音频）评估设备使用情况，并且可以在 "客户端 & 设备" 下的随附模板中找到。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1247">The device reports are used to assess device usage by volume and MOS score (audio only), and can be found in the accompanying templates under Clients & Devices.</span></span> 

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1248">除非你排除联盟参与者数据，否则这些报表将包含来自联合终结点的客户端遥测。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1248">Unless you exclude federated participant data, these reports will include client telemetry from federated endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1249">若要排除联合终结点，必须为设置为组织的[租户 id](#tenant-id)的**第二租户 id**添加查询筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1249">To exclude federated endpoints, you must add a query filter for **Second Tenant ID** set to your organization's [tenant ID](#tenant-id).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1250">或者，你可以使用[URL 筛选器](#url-filter)来排除联合参与者遥测。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1250">ALternatively, you can use a [URL filter](#url-filter) to exclude federated participant telemetry.</span></span>

> [!NOTE] 
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1251">请确保将 "月份年份" 筛选器调整为当前月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1251">Be sure to adjust the Month Year filter to the current month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1252">选择 "**编辑**"，然后调整**月份年份**以保存新的默认月份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1252">Select **Edit**, and adjust **Month Year** to save the new default month.</span></span>

> [!Note]
> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1253">您可能注意到查看此报告时，您看到的同一设备报告多次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1253">You might notice when viewing this report that you see the same device reported multiple times.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1254">这是由于向 CQD 报告设备的报告方式所致。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1254">This is due to the way the device is reported being reported to CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1255">硬件和操作系统区域设置的差异导致了设备数据的报告方式的差异。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1255">Differences in hardware and OS locale cause differences in how device data is reported.</span></span>
