<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1257">_图 31-设备（麦克风）报告_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1257">_Figure 31 - Devices (Microphone) Report_</span></span>

##### <a name="remediation"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1258">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1258">Remediation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1259">通常，你需要发现并阶段退出未验证的设备，并将其替换为经过认证的设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1259">Typically, you'll need to discover and phase out non-certified devices and replace them with certified devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1260">查看设备报表时的一些注意事项包括：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1260">Some considerations when reviewing the device reports include:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1261">适用于团队和 Skype for business 的设备是否已通过认证？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1261">Are the devices in use certified for Teams and Skype for Business?</span></span> 
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1262">你可以通过 "[呼叫分析](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309)" 标识特定设备的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1262">You can identify users of a specific device through [Call Analytics](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Skype-for-Business-Blog/Introducing-Call-Analytics/ba-p/57309).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1263">检查以确保它们具有最新的设备驱动程序，并且其设备未通过 USB 集线器或扩展坞连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1263">Check to make sure they have the latest device drivers and that their device isn't connected through a USB hub or docking station.</span></span> 
-   <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1264">不同的驱动程序正在使用多少个不同版本？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1264">How many different versions of various drivers are in use?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1265">他们是否定期进行修补？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1265">Are they being patched regularly?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1266">确保定期为音频、视频和 Wlan 驱动程序提供修补程序，有助于消除质量问题，使用户体验更具可预测性和一致性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1266">Ensuring that audio, video, and Wi-Fi drivers are being patched regularly will help eliminate these as a source of quality issues and make the user experience more predictable and consistent.</span></span>

##### <a name="audio"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1267">音频</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1267">Audio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1268">下一项任务是确定已[认证的音频设备](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs)的整体使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1268">The next task is to determine the overall usage of [certified audio devices](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1269">我们建议在所有音频流的至少80% 使用认证的音频设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1269">We recommend that at least 80 percent of all audio streams use a certified audio device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1270">最佳方法是将麦克风设备报告导出到 Excel 以计算认证或批准的设备的使用情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1270">This is best accomplished by exporting the microphone devices report to Excel to calculate the usage of certified or approved devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1271">组织通常保留所有已批准的设备的列表，因此对数据进行筛选和排序非常简单。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1271">Organizations typically keep a list of all approved devices, so filtering and sorting the data should be straightforward.</span></span>

##### <a name="video"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1272">视频</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1272">Video</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1273">视频驱动程序也很重要，您也可以继续更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1273">Video drivers are important to keep updated as well.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1274">确保视频卡定期修补有助于排除视频流质量不佳的视频驱动程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1274">Ensuring that video cards are being regularly patched will help exclude video drivers as a source of poor quality for video streams.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1275">使用[经过验证的视频设备](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs)有助于确保更平稳、高质量的用户体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1275">Using [certified video devices](https://partnersolutions.skypeforbusiness.com/solutionscatalog/personal-peripherals-pcs) will help ensure a smooth and high-quality user experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1276">支持 H-p 本机编码的视频设备是在视频会议期间减少 CPU 使用率的首选方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1276">Video devices that support H.264 native encoding are preferred, to reduce CPU usage during video conferencing.</span></span>

##### <a name="wi-fi"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1277">Wi-Fi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1277">Wi-Fi</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1278">Wi-fi 驱动程序还需要在常规节奏上进行修补，并且应包括在修补程序管理策略中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1278">Wi-Fi drivers also need to be patched on a regular cadence as well and should be included in your patch management strategy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1279">可通过维护最新的 Wi-fi 驱动程序来纠正许多质量问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1279">Many quality issues can be corrected by maintaining up-to-date Wi-Fi drivers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1280">有关优化 Wlan 基础结构的详细信息，请参阅[有关 wi-fi 计划的文章](/skypeforbusiness/certification/networking-wifi)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1280">For more information about optimizing your Wi-Fi infrastructure, see [this article about Wi-Fi planning](/skypeforbusiness/certification/networking-wifi).</span></span>

## <a name="appendix"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1281">参见</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1281">Appendix</span></span> 

### <a name="office-365-network-connectivity-principles"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1282">Office 365 网络连接原则</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1282">Office 365 network connectivity principles</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1283">在开始规划 Office 365 网络连接的网络之前，请务必了解安全管理 Office 365 流量和获得最佳性能的连接原则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1283">Before you begin planning your network for Office 365 network connectivity, it's important to understand the connectivity principles for securely managing Office 365 traffic and getting the best possible performance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1284">以下文章将帮助您了解安全优化 Office 365 网络连接的最新指南：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1284">The following article will help you understand the most recent guidance for securely optimizing Office 365 network connectivity:</span></span>

[<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1285">Office 365 网络连接原则</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1285">Office 365 Network Connectivity Principles</span></span>](https://aka.ms/pnc)

### <a name="planning-for-wi-fi"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1286">为 Wlan 进行规划</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1286">Planning for Wi-Fi</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1287">Microsoft 在无线网络中实现质量和灵活性的方法有三个部分：端到端的计划、部署中的最佳做法以及前瞻性的维护和操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1287">Microsoft's approach to drive quality and agility into the wireless networks comes in three parts: end to end planning, best practices in deployment, and proactive maintenance and operations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1288">此解决方案简述将指导你完成此过程以确保企业级的无线 Skype for business 体验：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1288">This solution brief walks you through this process to ensure an enterprise-class wireless Skype for Business experience:</span></span>

[<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1289">确保企业级的企业版 Skype for Business 体验</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1289">Ensuring an Enterprise Class Wireless Skype for Business Experience</span></span>](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=47257)

### <a name="lync-networking-guide"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1290">Lync 网络指南</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1290">Lync Networking Guide</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1291">有关团队和 Skype for Business 网络概念的更多背景以及对质量重要性背后的基本原理，请继续了解[Lync Server 2013 网络指南](https://blogs.technet.microsoft.com/nexthop/2013/06/03/lync-server-2013-networking-guide-network-planning-monitoring-and-troubleshooting-with-microsoft-lync-server/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1291">For more background on the Teams and Skype for Business networking concepts and rationale behind their importance to quality, the [Lync Server 2013 Networking Guide](https://blogs.technet.microsoft.com/nexthop/2013/06/03/lync-server-2013-networking-guide-network-planning-monitoring-and-troubleshooting-with-microsoft-lync-server/) is still applicable.</span></span>

### <a name="network-performance-requirements"></a><span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1292">网络性能要求</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1292">Network performance requirements</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1293">通过 IP 的实时媒体质量（音频、视频和应用程序共享）很大程度上受到端到端网络连接质量的影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1293">The quality of real-time media (audio, video, and application sharing) over IP is greatly affected by the quality of end-to-end network connectivity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1294">为获得最佳团队或 Skype for business 媒体质量，你的网络必须满足以下网络性能指标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1294">For optimal Teams or Skype for Business media quality, your network must meet the following network performance metrics.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1295">_表 12-网络性能要求_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1295">_Table 12 - Network performance requirements_</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1296">指标</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1296">Metric</span></span>                            | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1297">客户端到 Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1297">Client to Microsoft Edge</span></span>           | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1298">客户边缘到 Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1298">Customer Edge to Microsoft Edge</span></span>    |
|-----------------------------------|------------------------------------|------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1299">延迟（一种方法）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1299">Latency (one way)</span></span>                 | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1300">\<50 ms</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1300">\<50 ms</span></span>                            | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1301">\<30毫秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1301">\<30 ms</span></span>                            |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1302">延迟（RTT 或往返时间）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1302">Latency (RTT, or round-trip time)</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1303">\<100 ms</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1303">\<100 ms</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1304">\<60 ms</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1304">\<60 ms</span></span>                            |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1305">爆发数据包丢失</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1305">Burst packet loss</span></span>                 | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1306">\<在任何200毫秒的时间间隔内10%</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1306">\<10% during any 200-ms interval</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1307">\<1% 的任何200毫秒的时间间隔</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1307">\<1% during any 200-ms interval</span></span>    |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1308">数据包丢失</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1308">Packet loss</span></span>                       | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1309">\<在任何15秒的时间间隔内1%</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1309">\<1% during any 15-sec interval</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1310">\<任何15秒的时间间隔内0.1%</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1310">\<0.1% during any 15-sec interval</span></span>  |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1311">数据包内部到达抖动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1311">Packet inter-arrival Jitter</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1312">\<在任何15秒的时间间隔内30毫秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1312">\<30 ms during any 15-sec interval</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1313">\<任何15秒内的15毫秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1313">\<15 ms during any 15-sec interval</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1314">数据包重新排序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1314">Packet reorder</span></span>                    | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1315">\<0.05% 的订单外数据包</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1315">\<0.05% out-of-order packets</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="7e7f3-1316">\<0.01% 的订单外数据包</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7e7f3-1316">\< 0.01% out-of-order packets</span></span>      |
